Military Expenses for the North China Truce Somewhat Eased

(Tokyo) It is clear that the Saito Cabinet will compile the budget for the next fiscal year. When the previous parliament passed the budget for this fiscal year, it attached a serious resolution to the Saito Cabinet, demanding that it make efforts to establish a financial plan in the future. It is quite interesting to see how the current cabinet will compile the budget for the next fiscal year. The Manchurian Incident expenses and military equipment improvement expenses for this fiscal year total 400 million yen. However, based on the current situation in Manchuria, there is no possibility of reducing the Manchurian Incident expenses for the next fiscal year, and the military equipment improvement expenses will instead be doubled. In addition, there is hardly any room for reorganizing various established expenses. Therefore, the budget for the next fiscal year will increase compared to the 2.3 billion yen for this fiscal year. As for revenue, due to the gradual revitalization of the financial world, there is some hope for an increase in various consumption taxes and tariffs. The government's tax increase plan seems hopeless. Other tax increase plans include raising tobacco prices and postal fees. Regular annual revenue can be increased by about 50 million to 100 million yen compared to this fiscal year. However, comparing expenditures and revenues, expenditures are approximately 2.3 billion, while regular annual revenue is approximately 1.4 billion, and temporary revenue is 100 million, totaling 1.5 billion yen. After offsetting, there is still a shortfall of 800 million yen. This amount must be sought from public bonds, so a large amount of public bonds will also be issued next year. (4th, Japan United Press)

(Tokyo) As the political situation has stabilized, the Japanese government is focusing on the budget compilation period. The Ministry of Finance has already started preparing under the budget compilation policy. As Finance Minister Takahashi has moved to Hayama, the outline of the compilation policy should be decided within this month. Therefore, the cabinet will generally decide on the following policies in mid-month: Requests for new projects are limited to urgent ones. Each ministry should strive to save established expenses for new projects to replenish financial resources. The Manchurian Incident expenses, military equipment improvement expenses, and expenses for saving the current situation must be discussed separately. There is no difference between this and the budget compilation policy for the 8th year of Showa (1933). However, the difficulty this time is how to prevent the expansion of expenditures caused by the increase in military spending, which is the biggest reason, and how to fill the revenue deficit caused by the issuance of deficit public bonds. The former has been slightly eased due to the stability of the political situation in North China and the healthy development of "Manchukuo," but the replenishment of weapons and materials and the improvement of weapons will increase compared to the 8th year of Showa, so an increase in expenditures is inevitable. As for the latter revenue, it is necessary to find ways to increase it. Therefore, the Tax System Revision Preparation Committee is eager to create a concrete plan. However, the public is worried about the issuance of public bonds, but the government, due to the military's enthusiastic tax increase theory, Finance Minister Takahashi has recently inclined towards the tax increase theory. Therefore, the result will be to increase postage and cigarette prices, and to add sales taxes. (4th, Denstu)

(Tokyo) The Navy Ministry's budget for the next fiscal year is currently being reviewed by the Bureau of Accounting. Its total amount is approximately 400 million yen, of which the newly requested expenses include ship maintenance fees, aviation fees, land and sea equipment fees, warship defense fees, and various research fees. Another important issue is the Second Replenishment Plan established due to the London Treaty. Navy Minister Osumi stated in the previous parliament that this expense is necessary this year. According to the Navy Ministry's original proposal to the Ministry of Finance, the ships to be built are one defense ship (8,000 tons), two cruisers (8,500 tons), seven destroyers (1,400 tons), one mine-laying ship (5,000 tons), six submarines of various sizes, and several minesweepers and torpedo boats, totaling 370 million yen. The Navy authorities hope to complete them before the 11th year of Showa (1936). (4th, Japan United Press)

(Tokyo) The Kanto region's large-scale air defense exercise, which will be held in mid-August this year, is unprecedented in Japan. The Tokyo Garrison Command and the authorities of each prefecture have already decided on a concrete plan and are now preparing for it. Tokyo Garrison Commander Lieutenant General Hayashi is the exercise supervisor, the governors of each prefecture are advisors to the supervisor's office, and the police chiefs of each prefecture are members of the supervisor's office. The air defense headquarters is located in the Army Military Academy. Staff officers from the Yokosuka and Tateyama Naval Air Corps, the Army General Staff Headquarters, the Garrison Command, the Aviation Headquarters, and the Field Heavy Artillery School, and other relevant authorities for each exercise, held a final meeting the other day to discuss the methods for carrying out various air defense tasks. The attacking military planes are 30 planes launched from a naval aircraft carrier to attack the capital. The defending military planes are 50 planes from the army, and more than 30 anti-aircraft guns, sound locators, searchlights, etc. will also participate. When the attacking military planes arrive in Tokyo, the entire city will be blacked out. (Japan United Communications)

Japan Does Not Abandon Its Policy of Aggression, Opposes the Arms Reduction Convention and Security Guarantees 41

(Tokyo) The executive committee of the Geneva Arms Reduction Conference will discuss the proposal of British Prime Minister MacDonald. The Japanese government has issued a comprehensive instruction to its plenipotentiary, Sato, regarding the British proposal. This afternoon, it was strictly ordered that all clauses in the first part of the MacDonald proposal, which guarantees security, must not be agreed to under any circumstances. It was also ordered to state Japan's attitude at the executive committee meeting. The reasons are as follows: The first part of the MacDonald proposal stipulates that whether or not there has been a violation of the Non-Aggression Treaty will be decided by the contracting parties of the five powers after consultation. In order for it to take effect, it will be decided according to the Seven-Power Consultation Treaty of the UK, US, France, Italy, Japan, and Russia. However, it is difficult for Japan to participate, as its spirit is the same as withdrawing from the League of Nations. The third article of the first part stipulates that whether or not there is a threat to violate the Non-Aggression Treaty will be decided by a five-power conference. All procedures for the contracting parties to hold a meeting are determined by the Secretary-General of the League of Nations, and the meeting place is decided in principle in Geneva, which are all difficult for the Japanese government to accept. The Japanese government limits the intervention of third countries or the League of Nations in the political problems of the Far East. Therefore, it has broken ties with the League of Nations. Therefore, there is no room for reservation or amendment to the first part. Therefore, it will strictly adhere to the established policy of maintaining a free position outside of the agreement items for applying the first part. (4th, Denstu News Agency)

(Tokyo) After Japan withdrew from the League of Nations, the heads of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs carefully studied foreign policy. Recently, a plan has been formed, and the necessary expenses will be requested when the government compiles the budget for the next fiscal year to concretize and regenerate foreign policy. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs is currently conducting informal negotiations with the Ministry of Finance. It is heard that the diplomatic expenses will be used as follows: 1. The Empire's diplomatic plan after withdrawing from the League aims to expand and strengthen its national economic diplomacy. 2. For this purpose, consulates in places such as continental Europe where economic relations with Japan are not very close will be abolished or reduced, while the diplomatic organs in important markets for Japanese goods such as Egypt, South Africa, India, Southeast Asia, China, "Manchukuo," and the Americas will be expanded. 3. The trade relations between Japan and India are serious, and special measures should be considered. Currently, there are only the Consul-General in Calcutta and the Consul in Bombay in India. Next year, consulates should be established in Karachi and Madras, and an ambassador-level figure should be appointed as the Consul-General in Calcutta to negotiate all issues with the Indian government. (4th, Japan United Press)

US Senate Passes Bill to Abolish Gold Standard 64

Thirty-Six Countries Have Already Devalued Their Currencies

National News Agency, 3rd, Washington. Today, Republican Senator Borah led the gold standard supporters to a great victory in the Senate with the most vehement speech of his life. By a large majority of 48 votes to 20, the bill to abolish the gold standard was passed, causing only 20 Republicans, who have always been known for supporting the gold standard, to maintain their original position. The remaining 16 joined the Democrats' inflationary faction and voted to defeat the gold standard. Even with the best efforts of Virginia Senator Glass and Pennsylvania Senator Reed to defend the gold standard, they could only lament the inevitable trend of the times. The bill is now being sent to the White House, where the President is expected to sign and promulgate it immediately. From then on, all currencies in the United States will become "legal tender" and can be used to pay customs duties and other debts to the government, and the government can also use them to repay the principal and interest on public bonds. In legal terms, it is no longer necessary to have gold coins and gold certificates. After the bill was introduced to the Senate today, the opposition (i.e., the gold standard supporters) tried their best to amend it, limiting its application to future gold coin debts, arguing that Congress had no right to destroy obligations that had already been established. This amendment was also rejected by the majority because if it had been adopted, the government would still have had to use gold coins to redeem existing public bonds. Borah's most important point in the debate was that since 36 countries have already devalued their currencies, the gold standard cannot be maintained. These countries initially struggled to maintain it, but were ultimately forced by the trend of the times to abandon the gold standard.

American Speculative Fever 65

Differing Opinions from Various Parties

National News Agency, Washington, 3rd – The American public’s sudden return to the securities market and the increasing fervor of speculation is causing considerable concern to the government. There are widespread rumors that the President is considering a plan to curb the speculative fever, but inquiries at the White House have failed to confirm this. It is also reported that government advisors have warned the authorities that if a speculative wave does occur at this time, it will render much of the work of raising prices futile. However, according to news from New York, Chicago, and San Francisco, brokers and merchants are not paying much attention to this matter. New York financiers do not believe that the rise in the securities market will have a detrimental impact on business, and merchants are conducting business as usual. Most believe that the government cannot legally prevent the public from buying and selling securities, and they say that the recent rise in the securities market is not entirely the result of speculation, but largely due to rising prices. Furthermore, there is one thing that can ease the concerns of those in power: there is currently no movement to organize new companies, and no large-scale speculative securities have appeared on the exchanges.

German Economic Situation 66

Hopes for Improvement from the London Conference

National News Agency, Berlin, 3rd – The President of the German National Bank, Schacht, departed for Basel this evening to attend the meeting of the Bank for International Settlements convened on Sunday and Monday. After Schacht returns to Berlin from Basel, the German government will consider the issue of debt payments and the policies to be adopted. According to the Angriffe, the organ of the National Socialist Party, the current state of the debt payment issue is roughly as follows: "Due to the significant shortage of cash and foreign currency in the German National Bank, and the fact that restrictions on export trade have not been removed, the representatives of various countries at the payment conference agree that suspending payments is the only way out at present. Therefore, Germany's hopes for the World Economic Conference are twofold: first, that the various restrictions on German export business can be lifted as soon as possible; second, that a solution to the private debt problem can be found. If the London Conference can resolve these two issues soon, not only can Germany engage in economic construction, but it can also resume foreign debt payments. This is indeed the key to the common interests of all countries in the world."

Eastern European Alliance Conference 69

Havas, Romanian Capital, 4th – The conference of agricultural countries in Eastern and Central Europe opened today. The eight countries that decided to establish the "Eastern European Alliance" in 1930, namely Estonia, Latvia, Poland, Czechoslovakia, Hungary, Romania, Yugoslavia, and Bulgaria, have all sent representatives to participate. In addition, representatives from Greece and Turkey are attending the meeting as observers. The discussions at the meeting will focus on establishing a common program for agricultural countries in Eastern and Central Europe to be presented at the London Economic Conference. The main point of this program is the difficult situation of agricultural product exports caused by the worldwide overproduction of agricultural products. This program represents 100 million people, most of whom are engaged in agriculture. The conference will address the issue of providing long-term loans to agricultural countries. The agricultural countries plan to point out to creditor countries at the economic conference that it would also be beneficial to creditor countries if agricultural debtor countries were allowed to repay debts with agricultural products, as creditor countries would then organize markets to absorb the exports of debtor countries. Finally, the agricultural countries' conference will discuss the results of the preferential tariff rates agreed upon at last year's Dresden Conference, recognizing the need to protect them.

Spanish Anti-Religious Movement 72

Religious Courses Banned in Schools

Clergy Prohibited from Entering Universities

Reuters, Rome, 3rd – The Pope issued a notice today, strongly condemning the separation of church and state law in Spain and the church act that the Spanish president has now approved. This church act stipulates the confiscation of church property and prohibits Catholic clergy from teaching. The Pope urged Spanish Catholics to use their ability to promote the teaching of religious studies and to unite to defend their faith, but the notice implied that the church could cooperate with the government. The Pope did not order Catholics to overthrow the new government, saying that the church could recognize any political system, but freedom of belief must be completely unimpaired.

This move was unexpected by the church authorities, so church leaders everywhere have risen up in opposition, declaring that anyone who harms the church should receive appropriate punishment. It is feared that this will cause political and religious disputes in Spain, but it is generally believed that the church will not excommunicate the president. According to the new law passed by the parliament, all elementary schools established by various churches should be closed by October 1 of this year, and secondary schools established by churches should be closed by June 1 of next year. All clergy, monks, and nuns are not allowed to attend universities.

Reuters, Madrid, 3rd – The Spanish government's religious bill stipulates that Catholic priests are not allowed to carry out other educational activities except for theology. More than 4,000 monasteries and other religious institutions must now pay taxes, which they were previously exempt from. Anglo-Russian Trade After the Boycott 74

TASS, London, 3rd – Today, the Daily Herald published a detailed chart illustrating that Anglo-Russian trade has suffered a fatal blow since the British government's explicit boycott of Russian goods. The total value of orders placed by the Soviet Union in Britain reached £3,670,000 in the first five months of 1932, while in the same period this year it was only £700,000. In April 1932, the value of Soviet orders in Britain was £1,177,000, and in May it was £1,442,000, but in April this year, the total value of orders reached only £314,000, and in May, the Soviet Union placed no orders with Britain. The leasing of ships also shows the same decline. In April 1932, Soviet companies leased four ships, paying £189,000 in rent to British steamship companies, while last month, Soviet companies did not lease a single ship from Britain.

The British Emperor's Sixty-Eighth Birthday: No Special Celebrations for the Royal Family 75

Reuters, London, 3rd – The British Emperor celebrated his sixty-eighth birthday at Buckingham Palace today. The ceremony was simple, and there were no special celebrations for the royal family. Although the Emperor is still healthy, shoulder pain prevents him from riding a horse or wearing full military attire. Therefore, the Emperor's birthday parade was performed by the Crown Prince. The Emperor stood in the palace, looking down at the Prince leading the troops past. The weather was clear today, and there were more spectators than in previous years. Seeing the Emperor standing on the balcony, cheers erupted. The Emperor removed his hat, bowed, and waved to show his gratitude.

A Painful History of Overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia 76

Mine Owners and Foremen Exploiting and Abusing

Tens of Thousands of Chinese Laborers Displaced

(Reuters, Singapore Correspondence, 30th) Song Faxiang, the Chinese Consul-General in Java, returned from an inspection of West Borneo and vehemently condemned the cruel methods used by the mine owners and foremen of the Billiton Island and West Borneo tin mines to treat Chinese laborers. According to his statement, none of the Chinese laborers employed in the Billiton Island and West Borneo tin mines will be able to accumulate a small fortune or return to their homeland after their contracts expire under the current circumstances. This is because there is a major payment day every six months, when workers can withdraw all the wages they have saved with the owners, but most of them have already spent all their wages on daily expenses. Pre-paid expenses require interest of nine cents for every two and a half guilders. On the major payment day, the owner supervises the deduction of all pre-paid expenses and interest from China and Japan. Moreover, that day is also a Fantan day, and there are various forms of gambling, so the workers' remaining funds are often spent here. The factory owners exploit the workers with cunning plans. They set up stores that sell various dry foods and other items to the workers at extremely high prices. The workers only seek temporary convenience and do not care about the high prices. Over time, their debts accumulate and must be paid off in full on the major payment day. What is even more painful is that these stores also sell opium, so that the funds earned by the workers' blood and sweat are either spent on gambling or lost to drugs. It has been found that the tin mines and tobacco plantations in the two places employ tens of thousands of Chinese laborers. According to the contract, they receive wages of seven and a half guilders per day and must work at least 360 days to complete a one-year contract. Before the contract expires, they are not allowed to engage in other occupations. On average, workers need one and a half years to complete their contract, and the weaker ones need two or three years, because they are often plagued by illness and cannot work. After the first year of the contract expires, both parties can freely renew it for another year. The second-term wages are higher, between 15 and 30 guilders per month, but the foremen exhaust all means to make the workers pre-spend a large portion of their wages before the second contract expires, so that they cannot remit money back home or leave their jobs. It is said that among those who complete their first contract, less than one in a hundred is able to settle their debts with the owner before their death. Mr. Song is now doing his best to improve the situation of these unfortunate workers, and the Nanjing diplomatic government is handling the negotiations.

Public Telegram 77

To all newspaper offices in Guangzhou, The communist bandits in Jiangxi are being suppressed, but foreign troubles are taking advantage of the situation. The fate of the nation is hanging by a thread, and there is no time to delay. This is truly a time of national crisis. Jitang, holding a military rank, bears a heavy responsibility and fears that the Republic of China, which was built with great difficulty, will be destroyed, and that the noble Chinese nation will be reduced to servitude. I am restless day and night, unable to sleep or eat. Since the bandits have spread throughout the four borders, I have reluctantly deployed elite troops, led by General Yu Hanmou, to enter Jiangxi, all to eliminate the bandits and harm the people for the sake of the country. Since starting until now, it has been more than a year, and there have been hundreds of battles, large and small. Among them, the Battle of Chijiang Shuikou inflicted the heaviest damage on the bandit army. It is a pity that the Guangdong defense must also be taken into account, and it was not possible to increase the number of troops to pursue the victory, so the bandits were able to survive and continue their poisoning. Now, the people of Jiangxi who are trapped in the bandit dens cannot even seek death, and those who are fortunate enough to be outside the bandit area are also suffering from traffic congestion and food shortages, either committing suicide by jumping into the river or hanging themselves, or making cakes from soil to fill their hunger. The tragic state of displacement and death cannot be described in words. Alas, my people are suffering from this great disaster. Who is to blame? I cannot but hate the extremely vicious red bandits who are willing to be tigers. Now that the pacification work in Guangdong Province is gradually being completed, seeing the rampant bandits in Jiangxi and hearing the urgent border situation, I am doubly concerned in this difficult time. In addition to dispatching elite troops to the north to resist foreign aggression, I am planning to send additional troops to drive straight into Jiangxi and join forces with the other armies to encircle and suppress the bandits. Jitang has been appointed as the Commander-in-Chief of the Southern Route of the Jiangxi, Guangdong, Fujian, Hunan, and Hubei Bandit Suppression Army, and should do his best to eliminate the bandits and thugs, fight for the survival of the Party and the country, and seek a way out for the nation. As long as there is a breath left, I will not hesitate to turn back. Alas, Li and Zhang caused chaos in the Central Plains, and the Manchus took the opportunity to invade. The past is not far away, and the lessons are there. In the vast thousands of years, I think of the great difficulties of the future. In the vast China, I see the limited sunset. Without waving Lu Yang's spear, it is difficult to resolve the crisis of Huang Chao. I hope that the advanced members of the Party and the country, and the comrades in the army, will feel the danger of being in the same boat in the wind and rain, and strive to lie on firewood and taste gall, uniting our hearts and minds to overcome the difficulties together, so that we can eliminate the red disaster and resist foreign aggression. The future of the nation depends on this. I respectfully submit this telegram and await your instructions. Chen Jitang, Commander-in-Chief of the Southern Route of the Jiangxi, Guangdong, Fujian, Hunan, and Hubei Bandit Suppression Army, bows his head.

Xu Bandits Re-occupy Nanjiang Amidst Sichuan War 78

Tian Songyao and Liu Cunhou's Troops Both Suffer Losses

Liu and Deng Have Not Stopped Fighting, Sichuan Situation Becomes Increasingly Serious

Hankou Correspondence: Sichuan, anciently known as the Land of Abundance, has remarkable mountains and rivers, and abundant products. The Red Bandits have wanted to seize it for more than a day. Last December, Xu Xiangqian's bandit troops fled from Hubei to Shaanxi, approaching Hanzhong. General speculation was that they would flee towards Gansu. At that time, the garrison in Nanzheng was weak, and the defense of Gansu was even more empty. If they launched a fierce attack on Nanzheng, crossed the Han River, and crossed the Jialing River, it would not be difficult to drive straight in and achieve their wish. However, after reaching Nanzheng, they fled south. Before long, Tongjiang fell, and Nanjiang and Bazhong were also captured by them. Then it was known that the bandit's purpose was here and not there. After entering Sichuan, the bandits regarded it as a new base and spared no effort in its management. Northern Sichuan was originally barren, and the people had long suffered from harsh government. After being instigated by the bandits, many people joined them. Within a few months, pseudo county, town, district, and township Soviet governments were organized, and the bandit's strength increased from several thousand to tens of thousands. Chiang Kai-shek believed that the bandit's entry into Sichuan was a hidden danger and appointed Tian Songyao as the Bandit Suppression Supervisor of the Sichuan-Shaanxi Border Area, responsible for blocking and suppressing them. He also ordered Yang Hucheng, the Pacification Director stationed in Shaanxi, to send troops to pursue them. At this time, the Sichuan war had come to an end, and Tian dispatched five divisions of his six divisions to meet the enemy. Tian himself also went to Hanzhong to command. Liu Cunhou, the Border Defense Supervisor of Sichuan and Shaanxi, also sent heavy troops to assist. After several battles, the bandits were defeated, but they never intended to leave Sichuan. Recently, Liu Wenhui and Deng Xihou's cliques became enemies, and war was imminent. Because the bandits had not left the border, they did not dare to launch an attack. Xu Bandits, in order to promote the Sichuan war, immediately abandoned Tongjiang, Nanjiang, and Bazhong, and retreated into Shaanxi. Thus, the victory telegrams of bandit suppression came like snowflakes, but they did not know that they had fallen into their trap. After the rupture between Liu and Deng, three divisions of Tian's troops were sent to Deyang, Shifang, Pengxian, and Huaizhou to concentrate and participate in the war. Most of the garrison troops in northern Sichuan were old, weak, and incompetent. Xu Bandits, knowing that northern Sichuan was empty, immediately made a comeback. At the end of last month, they reached Kushu Dam in Tongjiang, defeating Tian's troops. Liu Cunhou's reinforcements were also defeated and could only hold on to the dangerous terrain. The bandits then attacked Nanjiang with large forces. It is reported that the county seat of Nanjiang was re-occupied on the 30th, and there is a tendency to disrupt Tongjiang, Wanyuan, and Bazhong on a large scale. Tian and Liu's troops have both suffered losses and seem to have no resistance. If reinforcements are not sent to counterattack, the counties in northern Sichuan may all be occupied by Xu Bandits. At this critical moment, the war between Liu and Deng has not stopped. On the 2nd, Liu's troops, led by Leng Yindong's division and Li, Song, Liu, Zhao, and Huang's brigades, launched a third general attack on Deng's army in Chongning and Sandao Yan. Huaizhou also launched an attack at the same time. The goal is still to cross the Kun River and capture Pengguan and other counties. It is also reported that the river embankment opposite Jinzhu Weir has been destroyed by landmines, and the farmland in the fourteen counties of western Sichuan has been flooded. The Sichuan warlords are harming the country and the people to such an extent that they are truly guilty and unforgivable. (3rd)

Kyoto Imperial University Student Unrest (Japanese Correspondence) 79

(Truth) What exactly is it that needs to be proven conclusively? In the natural sciences, it is easier to prove with more concrete facts. In the humanities and social systems, it is very difficult to determine. Even when the natural sciences have not fully convinced their opponents, there are still many examples of persecution. For example, the heliocentric theory is now a theory that no one will deny, but in the 17th century, Galileo's heliocentric theory offended the Bible and angered the French Emperor, and he was forced to swear in Rome that he would no longer write books advocating "geocentrism." Even in his old age, he could not avoid being imprisoned. Similarly, evolution is now almost considered an indelible truth, but at that time, even professors at British universities were expelled from their schools. The states of Tennessee and others in the American South even banned the study of evolution in public schools, facts that were ridiculed by the world's cultural circles. Thinking of Qin Shi Huang, the first emperor of our motherland, who wanted to unify the world and prepare a foundation for his sons and grandsons to rule for ten thousand generations, he implemented an extremely foolish policy, even resorting to "burning books and burying scholars" to maintain the unified world.

Since Hitler came to power in Germany, there has been one more fascist state. In order to stabilize its regime, it has not hesitated to imitate Qin Shi Huang, not only listing all writings with red and revolutionary meanings as against the national will and spirit, but also having the Brownshirts search everywhere, burn these books, and drive away all left-wing scholars. This is the case in the West, and of course, things cannot be too monotonous in the East. Japan has been the most sincere and similar country to Germany for decades, especially in learning from Germany militarily, which is a well-known story.

Although Japan has not suffered the serious post-war blows like Germany, burdened with reparations and bound by the Treaty of Versailles, it is making every effort to create a so-called national crisis, wanting to use force to open up economic avenues amidst the global panic. Therefore, it forcibly created the September 18th Incident, using military action to stimulate the military supplies industry, and ostensibly supporting the production index in a superficial balance. Moreover, because of the strict police and the unified action of the military and the press, almost no one outside Japan fully knows its true nature. The general public in Japan is also poisoned by "nationalism." Even those who are not poisoned dare not speak out. On the one hand, there is police surveillance, and on the other hand, there is the brute force of the rural veterans' associations. People who speak the "truth" have no opportunity to speak, and their writings are also difficult to make public. Culture will regress.

However, research within Japan is still relatively free. The Imperial University Library and other libraries still hold many banned books. There are still many professors at various universities who are searching for "truth." These people who are searching for truth, especially those who are searching for truth in the social sciences, are thorns in the side of the military authorities and are rebels against the current Japanese society. Kyoto Imperial University produced Kawakami Hajime, which was already earth-shattering, but in the general intellectual world, he has the authority of "truth" and wins the trust and admiration of the majority. Now there is the Takigawa Yukitoki professor incident. Professor Takigawa wrote a "Textbook on Criminal Law" a year ago. This book was originally not a very serious "traitorous" work. It merely criticized the shortcomings of Japan's current criminal law from a Marxist standpoint. Therefore, he was charged with offending the authorities and will be dismissed. The Ministry of Education explained Professor Takigawa's crimes as follows:

"First, regarding Professor Takigawa's writings on criminal law, his fundamental thought is Marxist thought, and he also admits that changes in the structure of the social economy are necessary. Second, regarding the crime of insurrection described in the 'Textbook on Criminal Law' (he admits that it is a revolution), it is harmful to the good customs of Japan. Third, Professor Takigawa's various writings, such as 'Textbook on Criminal Law' and 'Lectures on Criminal Law,' etc., are all harmful to security and destroy the purity and beauty of customs, thus violating the 'principle of cultivating students' personality and fostering national thought.' Therefore, the Ministry of Education advocated suspending Professor Takigawa to rectify the academic atmosphere."

However, the school, from the students to the president of the university, did not agree with the Ministry of Education's proposition. First, they argued that universities have academic freedom, and this freedom is conferred by law. Second, Professor Takigawa's writings have not in the slightest degree destroyed national thought or damaged the cultivation of students' personalities. On the contrary, they have precisely perfected this thought and cultivated students' loyal beliefs. Third, the Ministry of Education disregarded the autonomy of Kyoto Imperial University and overstepped its authority in dismissing Professor Takigawa's teaching position. Therefore, thirty-nine scholars, including all the professors, assistant professors, lecturers, and assistants of the Kyoto University Faculty of Law, jointly submitted their resignations, and President Konishi also submitted his resignation. At the same time, more than 1,600 students of the Faculty of Law united firmly to uphold "truth" and academic freedom and to resist the illegal oppression of the authorities. Not only the various faculties of Kyoto University showed sympathy and consistent support for the Faculty of Law, but other imperial universities were also brewing movements to sympathize with Kyoto University and oppose the Ministry of Education. Kyoto University graduates in cities such as Osaka and Tokyo are preparing for movements to uphold "academic freedom" and resist "government violence." Japanese schools have never had much unrest. This student unrest has very significant ideological implications and serious political implications. But let's see how this unrest unfolds. (May 30, 1933, in Osaka)

Developments in the Northern Situation: The Southwestern Anti-Japanese Bandit Extermination Army Temporarily Halts Its Advance 80

The 19th Route Army's Advance Contingent Temporarily Stays in Chenzhou

The Fourth Independent Division of Guangdong Sends Two Regiments to Pingshi and Lechang

Two Regiments of the Guangxi Army, Long and Ling, Are Transferred to Wuzhou for Training

The Southwestern Political Council Adds Military Ranks for Chen, Bai, and Cai

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Anti-Japanese Advance Contingent of the 19th Route Army, after leaving Guangdong Province and entering southern Hunan, has now reached Chenzhou and is temporarily resting. According to a telegram from the front yesterday, the First and Second Columns and the Headquarters of our army's advance contingent arrived in Chenzhou on the morning of the 25th. The weather was overcast and mild that day. They marched along the main road, and arrived in the afternoon. Thousands of male and female students from various schools in Chenzhou, representatives from various organizations, and people from all walks of life lined the suburbs to welcome them, with firecrackers and cheers, creating a very enthusiastic atmosphere. Commanders Zhang and Tan of the two columns arrived at the camping tents amidst the cheers. Furthermore, the Youth Service Corps, which accompanied the First Column northward, arrived in Chenzhou by car on the 25th and immediately started their propaganda work, which was quite effective in arousing the people. During this Corps's departure with the army, many people along the way requested to join the Corps's work, showing that the patriotic spirit of Chinese youth is not inferior to others. It is learned that after the two columns arrived in Chenzhou, they were ordered to rest temporarily in Chenzhou, and will await further orders before deciding whether to advance or halt. As for the Fourth Independent Division of Guangdong Province, after the First and Second Regiments were dispatched to Shaoguan, the First Regiment, led by Pan Biao, closely followed the tail of the 19th Route Army's advance contingent and has already arrived in Pingshi, while the Second Regiment, led by Zhang Haodong, has also been dispatched to Lechang. The Division Headquarters and the Third Regiment have not yet departed due to unfinished tasks. Furthermore, the 24th Division of the Anti-Japanese Army in Guangxi, led by Qin Lianfang, which was rumored to be transferred, had previously prepared to hire civilian boats to go east, but has not yet set off due to certain matters. According to a Wuzhou dispatch on the 24th, the 132nd Regiment of the 44th Division, led by Long Zhenyi, originally stationed in Pingnan County, has now been transferred to Wuzhou and Rongxu area for garrison. The vacated defense area is filled by teams dispatched from the 43rd Regiment, led by Liang Jin, originally stationed in Guiping and Yulin. The 133rd Regiment of the 45th Division, led by Ling Yaxi, originally stationed in Xixiangtang, Nanning, has also been transferred to Wuzhou for training. One battalion of Liang Jin's regiment in Guiping has been transferred to defend Rong County, and one battalion has been stationed in Pingnan, Teng County, Bahuo Xu, and other places. Recently, there has been a new development in the northern situation, so all armies have temporarily halted in the places they have reached. Unless there are major changes in the future, there seems to be no need for a hasty advance. The Southwestern Political Council, considering that Chen Jitang is determined to actively prepare to assume the position of Commander-in-Chief of the Southern Route of the Five Provinces Bandit Extermination, has used the name of the Council to grant Chen Jitang, Bai Chongxi, and Cai Tingkai military ranks. The order states: "In order to comply with the order, it is hereby noted that anti-Japanese and bandit suppression is the greatest proposition of this Council. In recent years, communist bandits have spread to the provinces of Jiangxi, Guangdong, Fujian, Hunan, and Hubei, and their poisonous flames have engulfed villages and markets. The armies of various provinces have repeatedly launched painful suppressions along different routes, but have not yet completely eradicated them. Now, although the country is in a time of difficulty, how can we resist foreign aggression and save the country from danger if we do not eliminate the scourge of communist bandits? It has been resolved by this Council to specially appoint Chen Jitang as the Commander-in-Chief of the Southern Route of the Jiangxi, Guangdong, Fujian, Hunan, and Hubei Bandit Extermination Army, Bai Chongxi as the Deputy Commander-in-Chief of the Southern Route of the Jiangxi, Guangdong, Fujian, Hunan, and Hubei Bandit Extermination Army, and Cai Tingkai as the Chief Commander of the Jiangxi, Guangdong, and Fujian Army Bandit Extermination Southern Route Forward. In addition to the separate orders, the appointment order is hereby issued. You are hereby ordered to lead the troops, inspire their morale, cooperate and conspire, and immediately launch an extermination campaign to eradicate the bandits at their roots, remove the blemishes, and fulfill the ultimate intention of this Council. We have high hopes." This order, (May 28th).

The Course of the Ceasefire Agreement: Tan Ya 81

Recently, the situation in the North has ended with a ceasefire, which is fortunate to have brought temporary peace. In reality, the opportunity for peace or danger hangs by a thread, and the key lies in the efforts made in one short hour at 22:00, which led to the mediation. Now that the Tanggu Agreement has been reached, North China can be supported for the time being. All the previous difficulties and obstacles have become history. Yesterday, a gentleman described the course of this matter in great detail, which is specially recorded below, perhaps it is also what the people of the country would like to hear.

The decision to have a partial ceasefire with Japan was made a month ago. At that time, the authorities realized that it would be difficult to win the war and that it would be futile to sacrifice lives, while those out of office also advocated taking a short respite and then planning to recover. After discussions among several people, a principle was decided. It was believed that some people in Japan also felt that it was impossible to annex North China through a long-term war, and that maintaining the puppet organization only needed the Great Wall line as sufficient, and the war could come to an end for a while. Under these two circumstances, some people began to run around in the name of private individuals. However, the army invading China belongs to the Kwantung Army, and although its overall policy towards foreign countries is consistent with that of Japan, there are also divisions within. Roughly speaking, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the military, and the Kwantung Army are three factions. As for the people who ran around on the other side, they were initially only from the foreign affairs department, belonging to the stream of intelligence propaganda. When they came, they were six parts propaganda and four parts sincerity, but their actual strength was only one part. They ran around north and south, scattering business cards, and both the government and the public saw them as private individuals. Seeing that China had many concerns, they said that the Japanese national character was able to yield and also to release, which was a legacy of the Yamato spirit, and that if they once released, there would be no complications. They also occasionally used the theory of race to advance their cause, and the intention of their propaganda was revealed in their words, and everyone knew it. Later, when Huang Fu came north, he first received the scope given by the government on this matter, and assisted the military in determining the standard for a ceasefire. The so-called scope meant that it could not involve politics or diplomacy, and that it must be purely a partial military agreement. If it was within the scope, he would handle it himself to protect Tianjin and Beijing; if it exceeded the scope, there would be no room for negotiation. When he went north, the bombing incident occurred at Tianjin Station, which we speculate was done by reactionaries. This is because the reactionaries believe that if there is a war in North China, the larger ones can attempt to establish a second puppet organization, and the smaller ones can organize plainclothes teams and disrupt the area. If a ceasefire is reached, these people will lose their basis, so they will spare no effort to sabotage it in order to achieve their conspiracy. After Huang Fu came, he first consulted with He Yingqin of the Military Council, showed him the government's policy and limitations, and assisted in the process. As a result, the sound of a ceasefire became louder day by day, and Tianjin and Beijing were in danger. The people were moving and migrating, and when they heard this, they were slightly more stable. However, the contact between the two sides could not be achieved quickly due to the route. Moreover, the extreme circuity and twists and turns, and the twists and turns of the situation, could not be resolved until 22:00 in the evening. The embassy also contacted various parties, but the Japanese soldiers on the east road had reached Lutai on the north road and had fallen into Miyun, and had seized Tongzhou. The air force had come in large numbers, and Tongping was less than forty miles apart. Moreover, the power plant, water supply, and electricity of the Beijing trams were all in Tongzhou. If there was a problem, the impact would increase, and people would become more disturbed. However, by the afternoon of the 22nd, the Tongzhou County Government and the Public Security Bureau had withdrawn, and the military was conscripting people everywhere to carry out defense work. Fearing the riots of plainclothes teams in the city, sandbags were placed along the way, and soldiers were sent to protect the Forbidden City. The chaotic situation can already be seen. Furthermore, on the morning of that day, it was widely rumored at the gate of the Japanese Embassy that Zhao Jingshi had stabbed a Japanese policeman with a knife. As a result, the Japanese side claimed that they were discussing a ceasefire, but now there were complications, which obviously showed that the Chinese people were not sincere, and the topic was getting further and further away. Therefore, the people in charge of the contact saw that the whole effort was about to be destroyed and disaster was imminent, so they spared no effort to facilitate it. Regarding the stabbing of the Japanese soldier, they said that the embassy area was not our responsibility, and that the Japanese residents in the East City were safe and sound, which could serve as evidence. Finally, late on the 22nd, our side happened to get a statement from the government, and the two sides met and spoke briefly and directly. First, they spoke of a ceasefire, because the situation was so urgent at this time that everything else could not be discussed. The main points of the verbal agreement were: (1) We will send people to Miyun to discuss specific measures, (2) They will send people to Beijing, (3) A ceasefire will be implemented immediately, and (4) A place will be determined to formally discuss the matter. After this agreement was reached, the Japanese soldiers accepted the order and did not advance. However, the next day, they continued to shell, so stopping the attack and stopping the advance were two different things. The Japanese first issued an order to stop the advance, so there was still a coda. At that time, our soldiers had already begun to retreat, and the military immediately sent Xu Zuyi to Miyun to discuss the specific details. Once the details were clear, the Japanese soldiers withdrew. At this time, our Tong County began to be taken over by the military, and the situation in Tangshan and Lutai was relatively relaxed. The plainclothes teams, because the Sino-Japanese war was about to cease, and they would have nothing to do, launched riots for days, but ultimately achieved nothing. After Xu returned, the Japanese also sent people, and the decision to hold a meeting in Tanggu on the 29th was made. As for our principles, they had also been told to the other side, that if they were sincere in wanting a ceasefire, then anything outside our scope would have no results if raised. At that time, the Kwantung Army also knew that if they wanted to talk about a ceasefire, they could not force others to do what they could not do, so they were able to mutually understand each other's intentions in advance. On the 29th, our military officially sent people in a special train to Tanggu, and a group from the Kwantung Army also arrived on a warship at the agreed time. However, because they had contacted each other beforehand, all the wording was carefully considered to avoid involving other matters, so no complications arose temporarily. The next day, an agreement was reached and signed, and our representatives returned to Beijing that evening to receive the comfort of the Military Council the next day. Now that the terms of the ceasefire have been set, North China can be temporarily secured. However, the issues of maintaining order in the contested area and the mixed forces of the puppet state cannot be resolved overnight. There are still many things that need to be properly handled after this ceasefire. Our government has repeatedly stated that it has nothing to do with politics or diplomacy, but our nation cannot forget to recover. If we only seek temporary peace and become complacent, then the past of the Southern Song Dynasty will inevitably lead to defeat and destruction. A certain gentleman said, Confucius said that the people are spared but have no shame. Now that we are spared, what about the shamelessness? Although this is a joke, it has great truth and is enough to be a head-on blow for our Chinese people. After the ceasefire agreement was announced in the newspapers on June 1, the people of the north were greatly relieved. As a result, the state of military affairs is gradually disappearing, and the Political Committee is actively preparing, which can also be gradually achieved. From early establishment, only the rest of the broken North China, especially the counties in Hebei that were affected by the war, suffered huge losses. The reorganization of political affairs, once it begins, the handling of its busy and difficult tasks is no less than military affairs.

General Mobilization for Bandit Extermination in Hunan, Hubei, Henan, and Anhui Provinces 82

New Plans Decided at the Second He-He Meeting in Changsha

Liu Zhenhua Arrives in Hankou to Take Office and Then Goes to Huangchuan

Hankou Correspondence: Since the signing of the ceasefire agreement, the attention of the Chinese people has focused on the issue of bandit suppression. The so-called "to resist foreign aggression, we must first pacify the interior" has become a unanimous slogan of the government and the public. At present, the areas where the bandit forces are most rampant are Jiangxi Province, followed by Hubei. The borders of Hubei, Henan, and Hubei are the main forces of the Red Bandits. In addition to supervising the suppression in Jiangxi, Chairman Chiang has tasked Xu Yuanquan with eliminating the He bandits, He Jian with eliminating the Kong bandits, Liu Zhenhua with eliminating the Kuang bandits, and He Chengjun with sitting in Hankou and taking care of all parties. He was entrusted with this important task, so he went to Shashi on the 29th of last month to meet Xu Yuanquan, went to Hunan on the 31st to meet He Jian, and returned to Hankou on the 2nd of this month to meet Liu Zhenhua. There have been the latest decisions on the bandit suppression plans of all parties. Now Xu and He (Jian) have all taken up their new positions, and Liu has also arrived in Hankou. The armies of all routes will simultaneously issue a general suppression order within days. The meetings of the past few days and the talks between He and Liu are recorded separately below.

(Changsha Meeting) The Chief of the Hubei Pacification Headquarters, He Chengjun, was ordered by Chairman Chiang to go to Hunan on the 31st of last month to swear in He Jian as the Commander-in-Chief of the Western Route of the Five Provinces Bandit Suppression Army, and to consult with Commander-in-Chief He on bandit suppression military affairs. He Jian's special train arrived in Changsha at 8:00 am on the 1st and participated in He's inauguration ceremony at 10:00 am. He then discussed with He Jian and generals Liu Jianxu, Li Jue, Wang Dongyuan, Chen Guangzhong, Tao Guang, Peng Weiren, and Liu Yinggu about the progress of the bandit suppression on the borders of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi. The principles decided by the two He's in Hankou in mid-April were followed, and slight changes were made in light of recent trends. He also reported the details of the Shashi meeting and asked Liu Jianxu to relay to his subordinates and to Xu Yuanquan's army to take contact and make an agreement on suppressing, so that the He bandits could not take care of both ends. It turned out that a part of Liu's army was also under the command of Xu Yuanquan, and He's earnestness in this matter was to achieve the effect of a pincer attack as soon as possible. He stayed in Hunan for only nine hours, because he had made a prior appointment with Liu Zhenhua to meet in Hankou on the 2nd, and it was inconvenient to delay, so he took a special express train from Hunan at 5:00 pm on the 1st and returned to Hankou. He did not inspect the troops along the way. At 8:00 am on the 2nd, the train arrived in Wuchang. He got off the train and changed ferries to cross the river and went directly to the Pacification Headquarters to work. He made a statement to reporters, saying, "I was sent by Chairman Chiang to Hunan to participate in the inauguration ceremony of Commander-in-Chief He Yunqiao. I met with Hunan generals such as Liu Jianxu and Li Jue in Hunan. There are already meticulous plans for suppressing the remaining bandits. All the generals will return to their defenses separately on the 2nd. Commander-in-Chief He is responsible for the important task of supervising the suppression of the Western Route, and is now coordinating the military and setting off for Pingxiang within days to command. The headquarters will be set up in Changsha, and an advance camp will be set up in Pingxiang to control the situation. He is prudent in his work, and the bandit suppression can be optimistic in the future. Because General Commander Liu Xueya was passing through Hankou on his way to Henan, I returned to Hankou to wait for him. After meeting with him, I will go to central and eastern Hubei to inspect."

(Hankou Meeting) The Commander-in-Chief of the Bandit Suppression in the Henan-Hubei border area, Liu Zhenhua, said that the Red Bandits in the Henan-Hubei border area were rampant and needed to go to Huangchuan to supervise the suppression, and needed to consult with Director He Chengjun and Chief of Staff Cao Haosen of the Headquarters on everything, so he took a postal flight from Anqing to Hankou at 2:00 pm on the 2nd. When he arrived in Jiujiang, the plane was damaged and landed in Xunyang. That night, he changed to the Dehe wheel and went west. He arrived in Hankou at 3:00 pm on the afternoon of the 3rd. That night, Director He hosted a banquet to wash the dust, and then Liu, He, and Cao had a meeting. Dai Minquan, commander of the 45th Division, Song Tiancai, commander of the 75th Division, Shangguan Yunxiang, commander of the 47th Division, representing Chu Hongjun, Zhang Ping, commander of the 30th Army, representing Zhang Ziping, Liu Gangfu, representing Wei Lihuang, commander of the Bandit Suppression in Eastern Hubei, and Hao Mengling, commander of the 54th Division, representing Xue Yuzhen, also went to pay their respects and ask for instructions. It is heard that the result of the Liu, He, and Cao meeting was to comply with the order of General Chiang to eliminate the Red Bandits in the border area of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui within three months. The deployment of the troops was largely the same as the decision made at the Hankou Bandit Suppression Meeting on the 8th of last month, but the pursuit and interception were adjusted according to the environment and adapted to the situation. Liu was originally scheduled to go to Huangchuan on the 4th, but it has now been decided to take office in Hankou. Liu told reporters, "The headquarters for bandit suppression in the border area of the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui has been arranged in Huangchuan, and the troops east of the railway have also been properly deployed according to orders. I will go to Huangchuan to supervise the suppression after taking office in Hankou, determined to follow General Chiang's intention to eliminate the remaining bandits in three months and handle the aftermath in six months. I have come here to consult with Director He and Chief of Staff Cao on how to proceed. There are meticulous plans for the suppression, and the primary task of the aftermath is to stabilize the people's hearts, because the people's hearts must be stable before the aftermath can be started. As for my concurrent position in Anhui's political affairs, I will be fair in employing people, and strive to save money in financial management. Other construction and education matters will also be based on benefiting the country and the people. After I leave, the provincial government will be represented by Ma Lingfu, the director of the Department of Civil Affairs. I will not return to Anhui until the small bandits on the three borders are eliminated." (3rd)

(Suzhou) Reactions to the Levying of the Fishery Construction Donation: The Fresh Fish Trade Association and the Embroidery Industry Association of Wu County believe that the Fishery Construction Donation Collection Office has violated the ministry's orders and arbitrarily sent police to forcibly collect the fishery construction donation, which is deemed illegal and disturbing. The fishermen are unable to bear the burden. They specially presented a request to the Ministry of Industry yesterday (4th), requesting strict orders to stop the forced collection, and requesting a prompt investigation to prevent Suzhou merchants, etc. Before the Ministry's order is received, all fish shops will temporarily suspend the collection on behalf of the office.

(Wuxi) The Fourth Day of the Cocoon Market Opening 83

Yesterday was the fourth day of the spring cocoon market opening. The price of fresh cocoons received by cocoon shops in various villages still varies greatly. Villagers in places such as Shitangwan will not sell cocoons unless they reach a certain price, so the cocoon price in that area has risen to 60 yuan. In other places such as Zhangjingqiao, Yuqi, Zhouxinzhen, Qianqiao, Huadafangzhuang, Dongfangqian, and Hudai Rihuibiao, the highest cocoon price is around 50 yuan, and the wholesale price ranges from about 42-43 yuan to 48-49 yuan. However, the cocoon price in Nanqiao is the cheapest, with the highest price being 40 yuan and the wholesale price being 38 yuan. The goods arriving in various villages are all booming. The Guangcheng cocoon shop in Yanqiao suddenly closed its scales yesterday afternoon, causing disputes. Yesterday, Zhenhua and another cocoon shop also reported their opening, for a total of 219 shops. Tan Xihong, Director of the Forestry and Reclamation Department of the Ministry of Industry, and Dong Xiujia, Director of the Jiangsu Construction Department, are paying close attention to the cocoon market in this county. They are deeply afraid that cocoon merchants will release their positions and indiscriminately collect cocoons. Yesterday, they specially ordered Yan County magistrate to pay close attention. In addition, the business tax of the cocoon shops in this county was originally handled by the Construction Bureau. Now that the Construction Bureau has been abolished, it is handled by the technicians' office of the county government. In addition to sending Ding to be stationed in the cocoon industry association, Zhang Fulin, the director of technology, also sent a letter to the association requesting a copy of the reported cocoon shops for verification. The original tooth tax has now been renamed cocoon shop business tax, with each shop paying one yuan. There is also a business special tax, with each stove also paying one yuan. The business tax is filled out by the technology office itself.

(Zhenjiang) Anhui Rice is Allowed to be Shipped Based on Letters 84

The Jiangsu Provincial Government previously approved the telegram from the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Administration, stating that Anhui rice and cattle transported through the Beijing-Shanghai Railway were repeatedly detained by military police along the way due to misunderstandings. The Deputy Director of the Transportation Department, Yuan Shaochang, was sent to the Provincial Government Secretariat and the Construction Department to discuss the matter. It is now proposed to instruct the military and police along the Beijing-Shanghai Railway to verify the special tax vouchers issued by the counties for the transportation of cattle passing through Anhui Province. The disabled old cattle and farming cattle purchased in Jiangsu Province, which are transported by train to and from the province, are also not subject to the ban on transportation and must be verified and released at any time to avoid misunderstandings and detention. It was approved by the 579th meeting of the Provincial Government Committee, and it was resolved that rice is allowed to be shipped, and cattle will be handled separately. The Provincial Government has now ordered the Civil Affairs Department to transfer instructions to the police along the Beijing-Shanghai Railway to comply with the regulations. In the future, Anhui rice transported by boat, arriving in Zhenjiang along the river, and not transferred to factories or warehouses, and directly transferred to trains for transportation, does not require a passport from this government, and should be verified and released based on the certification letter from the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce, and a letter should be sent to the Commander of the Military Police for verification.

(Bengbu) Garrison Troops Defeat Bandits 85

In the southern section of the Jinpu Railway, bandits have recently appeared from time to time, disturbing the local area. A group of more than two hundred bandits suddenly rushed to the east of Xinqiao Station north of Bengbu, hoping to loot. The director of the Jinpu Railway Police Section, Qi, heard the alarm and immediately reported to Wang Kaizhen, the regimental commander of the 37th Regiment of the 19th Brigade of the 7th Division, requesting that a team be sent to suppress them. After receiving the report, Wang immediately sent the entire 3rd Battalion of his troops to suppress them last night (2nd) at 12:00 pm. According to reports, the bandits have been defeated.
