Shen Bao Pharmaceutical Weekly 143

A Bird's-Eye View of Medicine and Pharmaceuticals in Shanghai in the Last Ten Years 144

— Pang Jingzhou

Chapter Four: Business Conditions

Section Four: Old Doctors and Traditional Chinese Medicine 145

Old doctors do not establish hospitals. All patients are treated in outpatient clinics or house calls. Therefore, when it comes to a few popular doctors, the number of patients they treat daily is often astonishing. For example, there is an old pediatrician in Shanghai who sees nearly one hundred patients every day. Each outpatient visit takes only three minutes. While taking the pulse, the students have already written the prescription. His business is so prosperous that the place is already crowded before dawn. Because he charges double for those who want to be seen first, an interesting thing happened. Many people take a child to see a doctor, pay two yuan to register early in the morning, and wait outside. If a child who arrives later has a more serious condition and is anxious to be seen first, they sell their number for three yuan. In this way, if their own child needs to see a doctor, they only spent one yuan. If they simply go home without seeing a doctor, they actually earn one yuan. So, a certain doctor's number has become a valuable security. The outside of his clinic has become an exchange. It can be considered a strange tale. And that doctor can truly be proud.

There is also a gynecology expert in the city who sees more than one hundred patients every day. Each prescription takes no more than three to five minutes. It is said that they can tell the sex of the fetus. I don't know if the statistics are accurate.

There is also a hereditary throat specialist who mostly uses diphtheria antitoxin and scarlet fever antitoxin. They also see about one hundred patients every day. I have personally seen them press the patient's tongue with their right hand to look at the throat while using their left hand to look at a boil on a child's head. And they are still shouting out the names of the medicines, ordering the students to write prescriptions. Meanwhile, several other students are giving antitoxin injections for them. However, the people waiting for treatment outside are still crowded. Therefore, there is an iron gate in his home to maintain order.

Some people think that the above situation is mysterious. In fact, it is only caused by people's excessive worship of experience, plus many blind followers. But naturally, some people in society do not agree with these hasty doctors. So, on the contrary, there are a few doctors who limit themselves to seeing twenty patients a day. No more after that. If you are late, you will not be seen. On the one hand, they raise their consultation fees several times to show the price of their day's mental concentration. Crossing the bridge and going beyond the boundary costs twenty or thirty yuan. They actually get the sympathy of society. Now, if we want to talk about the truth of old doctors' business, we cannot take the above people as representatives. The above is only about the business methods of these few people and their personal luck. As for the business development of most old doctors in general, we can still see it from the number of pharmacies. It can be said to be very developed. And the reason is that people's habits and knowledge are closer to old doctors and not close to new doctors. There is a very obvious example that can prove it. In my clinic, I still have one or two patients every month who do not know how to take new medicine. Often, I give them a prescription written from right to left, and they still ask, "Doctor, should I buy this prescription from a traditional Chinese medicine store and decoct it?" I must explain it to them again before they leave. With my limited business and the clear color of new medicine, and Shanghai being such an open city, there are still patients like this. This shows how deep the general public's concept of old medicine is, and on the other hand, it shows that the business of new medicine in the past has not penetrated the people. Then, the business of old medicine still occupies a large part. As for the so-called struggle mentioned above, it is still the struggle between old doctors and new doctors in the knowledge class.

Respectfully Informing the People of the Nation About Mr. Yu Ziwei's Will to Dissect the Remains (Part Two) Yu Yunxiu 146

The second example is the younger sister of my good friend, Mr. Lin XX, who is about fifty years old this year. She has always been a spinster, serving her old mother, and is enthusiastic about education, sparing no effort. She is a very admirable lady. She originally had stomach problems, which increased last year. According to X-ray diagnosis and various clinical diagnoses, it was also stomach cancer. Later, she vomited very badly, and she said that the vomiting seemed to originate from her neck, not from her stomach. According to the doctor's examination, it seemed that there was a slight swelling in the neck, but they thought that the vomiting was caused by pyloric stenosis caused by stomach cancer, so they did not pay much attention to the swollen part. Later, it got worse and worse, and she was dying. Suddenly, a monk came and said that he had medicine to cure it. The method was to starve a cow for two days and then give it bitter Chinaberry root bark to chew. Many sticky saliva would come out of the cow's mouth. They took this saliva and poured it into the patient's mouth. Who knew that after one dose, she vomited a lot, vomiting out a lot of pus. From then on, although the vomiting did not stop completely, it improved a lot, and the person gradually became more active. So, it spread as a miracle in the countryside. Some said that a single remedy could kill famous doctors, and some said that the Buddha had manifested. Because Ms. Lin believed in Buddhism. There were different opinions. Not long after, I suddenly heard that she had passed away. I asked what disease she had died of. They said it was pneumonia, and it only took three days. When I heard about this, I always had a lot of questions. Later, when I met Dr. Chen XX, because he had treated her several times, I asked him in detail. He said, "The monk did cure the disease a lot, but I think that the patient's severe vomiting may have been caused by an abscess in the neck, which stimulated the vomiting center in the medulla oblongata. When the cow saliva was taken, the time for the abscess had matured, and it happened to coincide. After vomiting a lot, the abscess broke through in the throat and esophagus, and a lot of pus was discharged. After that, of course, food could also be swallowed, the stimulation was reduced, and the vomiting was alleviated. Naturally, the body gradually felt better. As for stomach cancer, I am afraid it has not been cured." I think this explanation is very reasonable. I also asked him, "Is it really true that she later died of pneumonia?" He said, "I don't know the details, but I heard that she died quickly." I said, "It only took three days after the onset of the disease. If it was pneumonia, it would definitely not be so rapid. Perhaps the stomach cancer has not been cured. Due to fatigue and other reasons, a sudden massive hemorrhage occurred. When a lot of blood came out, there would naturally be symptoms such as shortness of breath and wheezing. Others thought it was pneumonia, but it is also possible." Dr. Chen said, "Perhaps it was a stomach perforation that caused peritonitis." Dr. Chen and I discussed and ended it there. We can no longer do further research. I think in this case, if a pathological autopsy could be performed, all kinds of questions could naturally be solved easily. Even the myth of the Buddha manifesting could be eliminated. Now, without real evidence to prove it, this mystery will never be revealed. It really makes me feel depressed and regretful.

From the second fact, we can know that without a pathological autopsy, there will never be any progress in disease prevention and treatment. "To cure the disease, one must seek the root." This sentence has never been absent in our precious Chinese "Inner Canon." "Using medicine is like using soldiers, knowing yourself and your enemy, you will win every battle." This theory has often been read in our precious country's medical books, but saying it is just saying it, but no one has ever actually done the work of "seeking the root" and "knowing the enemy." It is not that we don't want to do it, but there is no way to actually do it. Of course, the equipment is not enough, but the first is that there is no pathological autopsy, so there is no way to think about it. We can only blindly say what the ancients said, regardless of three or seven twenty-one, and deeply believe in it. And we create the saying that ancient sages were "born knowing," thinking that people like Shennong and the Yellow Emperor had supernatural intelligence and could understand thoroughly without actually studying the human body, so what they said was not wrong at all. We later people are ordinary mortals and are only worthy of following what the ancients said, not worthy of doubting the ancients' words again. This kind of thinking is actually a dead end, so we have to use these words to comfort ourselves, deceive ourselves, and by doing so, we can stabilize society and secure our rice bowls. This whole performance was a temporary strategy thought of by cunning people. Who knew that it would be passed down from generation to generation, and a hundred or so fools would seriously take it as the truth, creating a religious-style medicine. From then on, the work of "seeking the root" and "knowing the enemy" was devoted to studying books. So, wind, fire, summer, dampness, Shaoyin, Taiyang, kidney deficiency, liver exuberance, were talked about in a colorful manner, but the actual situation was not mentioned at all. For example, kidney deficiency, where exactly is it deficient? Is it anemia, atrophy, tuberculosis, or tumor? We don't care about any of them. We only rely on symptoms such as thinness and weakness, sore waist and seminal emission, to conclude that it is kidney deficiency. We randomly use ginseng, Rehmannia and other medicines to treat kidney deficiency. For example, dampness, what exactly is the essence of dampness? Is it water? Is it mucus? Is it the result of inflammation seeping out? Or is it the result of circulatory disorders leaking out? We don't care about any of them. We only rely on symptoms such as heavy head, weak stomach, and lazy limbs to conclude that it is dampness. We randomly use Atractylodes, Pinellia, Poria and other medicines to strengthen the spleen and dispel dampness. This kind of method of diagnosing and treating diseases is completely empty in the final analysis. Where is there even a trace that is close to the actual disease? So, there is never a possibility of "seeking the root" and "knowing the enemy." In other words, we will never know the disease, and we will never know the real method of treating the disease. After modern scientific medicine came in, in order to struggle for the door and for the sake of "seeking the root" and "knowing the enemy," old doctors did not dare to say anything anymore. Because saying it would only expose their ugliness, expose their shortcomings, and destroy their foundations. So, they hid it so tightly that not a word leaked out, so that the general public could continue to be deceived. Furthermore, they would say ugly things and spread rumors about the pathological autopsy work of scientific medicine, saying that it was digging people's eyes and sucking people's blood, or that it was cruel, inhumane, and not close to human feelings. They did not welcome, promote, or imitate their own pathological autopsy work. Unexpectedly, they turned around and played out a series of jealous, mocking, and disruptive behaviors. It is really unprogressive and not good.

Scientific Research on Cleanliness (Continued) 147

— Guo Renji

Scientific cleanliness is the foundation of health. There must be sufficient academic reasons. Relying only on shallow common sense based on customs and habits is not enough. In today's advanced medicine, all causes of health obstacles are clear. Today's cleanliness movement aims to eliminate causes harmful to health. Cleanliness is based on the foundation of etiology, with the goal of preventing disease. Therefore, it must be carried out. It is necessary to shift from subjectively perceived cleanliness to scientific cleanliness, and to study its uncleanness from a hygienic standpoint, divided into two types: chemical uncleanness and biological uncleanness.

Chemical Impurity 148

Some people who apply powder to their faces suffer from lead poisoning. This is an example of chemical impurity. Drinking water containing lead causes poisoning. This water is chemically impure. Eating puffer fish and dying is also because the food contains chemical impurities. Also, food that is prone to spoilage contains harmful preservatives, such as beverages. These are all chemically impure and unclean. The air contains a harmful gas, carbon monoxide, which is also a type of chemical impurity. Clothing contains harmful pigments.

Page 14

It is also equally unclean. Anything that can cause poisoning can be considered a chemical impurity.

Biological Impurity 149

Tapeworm larvae live in trout. People get sick from eating it. This trout is an unclean thing. Although the appearance of vegetables is clean, if their leaves are attached with roundworm eggs or typhoid fever bacteria, they should also be regarded as unclean objects. A small well is considered dangerous. Usually, its chemical composition is bad, which is harmful to the body. However, if typhoid bacteria are mixed in it, it is even more dangerous. It is not suitable for drinking if it is checked and found to contain ammonia. It is not that ammonia is a poisonous substance that cannot be used for drinking. The reason is that ammonia is mostly generated in toilets. Water containing this ingredient is feared to be connected to the toilet, so there is danger. The reason why the mixing of feces into water causes danger is that the danger does not belong to chemical danger. If the feces contain typhoid bacteria, dysentery bacteria, etc., these bacteria enter the mouth with the water, so there is danger. This is the so-called biological danger. However, boiling this dangerous well water for disinfection can ensure safety. And boiling water containing ammonia slightly will cause the ammonia to dissipate, so it can be reused.

The so-called biological impurity refers to the meaning of the danger of disease caused by the mixing of pathogenic bacteria and parasitic eggs. For example, the phlegm of patients with lung disease is dangerous because it contains tuberculosis bacteria. The phlegm of healthy people does not contain this bacteria, so it is not dangerous. Therefore, although the phlegm of healthy people is dirty, it is not dangerous. If the phlegm of patients with lung disease is boiled and sterilized once, although the appearance is dirty, it is still not dangerous. Although it is all phlegm, it is not biologically impure. The same is true for large and small stools. If the large and small stools of patients with infectious diseases are boiled and disinfected, they are not dangerous even if they enter the mouth. Although they are unclean and dirty in appearance, they do not affect human health. There is no need to pay too much attention to them. Although the appearance is not abnormal, from a scientific point of view, those who can be the cause of disease must be deeply vigilant. That is, the implementation of cleanliness needs to be scientific. What is the key to scientific cleanliness? It is said that if it is chemical, it is diluted. If it is biological, it should be disinfected. No matter how poisonous it is, it becomes harmless when diluted with water. No matter how dangerous it is, such as plague bacteria and cholera bacteria, the danger can also be eliminated by sterilization with heat or chemicals. It is essential to apply this scientific knowledge to seek thorough cleanliness.

Relief Methods for Farmers' Health 150

— Ding Fubao

In recent years, farmers have been on the verge of bankruptcy. Bankruptcy leads to inadequate food and clothing. To talk to them about hygiene is quite difficult. Here, I will discuss the most economical and effective new methods of hygiene.

If one is partial to various types of animal foods, the body will inevitably become ill. This is because meat lacks vitamins, calcium, and carbohydrates. Furthermore, meat accumulates waste products from the animal and toxins resulting from animal diseases, as well as decomposition after slaughter. Therefore, those who exclusively eat meat must excrete large amounts of waste and toxins. Over time, the kidneys will become inflamed, and the liver and heart will also become diseased. Headaches, constipation, and mental fatigue will occur. Blood vessel walls will thicken, arteries will harden, and gout will develop throughout the body. Moreover, there is the risk of parasites in meat. If one is partial to various types of plant foods, the body will become increasingly healthy. This is because vegetables, fruits, rice, and wheat contain various vitamins, calcium, and carbohydrates. Also, vegetarians have the greatest endurance, and they recover more easily after illness. Digestion is also easier compared to meat. This is the theory of Dr. Miller from the United States. I have not eaten meat since the age of forty-five, and it has been sixteen years now. I feel that my body and mind are improving every day. I continue to handle daily tasks as usual and have never stopped working due to illness. Therefore, my first recommendation to farmers is to be vegetarian year-round, which can save a significant amount of money.

White rice lacks the second type of vitamin because the bran has been removed. As a result, it loses a great deal of nutrients. Eating it often leads to beriberi. Therefore, we should eat brown rice, which has not had the bran removed. Brown rice contains the most nutrients. Farmers are unaware of this principle and use the most valuable part of the food, the bran, to feed pigs, which is truly a pity. A certain Japanese doctor has been vigorously promoting the consumption of brown rice, stating that if one spends ninety yuan on white rice, one can spend only sixty yuan by switching to brown rice. According to this, we know that eating brown rice is not only rich in the second type of vitamin but can also save one-third of the cost of rice. Therefore, my second recommendation to farmers is to eat brown rice year-round, which can save a significant amount of money.

The new hygiene method of Mr. Fletcher from the United States advocates frugality in eating and chewing thoroughly, which is greatly beneficial for health. The method is as follows: Only eat when genuinely hungry, one. All food must be chewed carefully, until it is thoroughly broken down, and then swallowed, two. Focus the mind while eating, paying attention to the mouth, observing how it is being chewed, how it is mixing with saliva, and what flavors are emerging. In this way, there is sufficient saliva to stimulate the gastric glands, resulting in abundant gastric juices. This makes food easier to digest. Digestion leads to easy absorption. Absorption leads to a feeling of fullness, and one can stop eating. Stopping eating must be guided by the natural feeling of satisfaction. If one eats until the stomach is full and the abdomen is distended, feeling uncomfortable, it is truly inappropriate, three. By strictly adhering to the above three points, the necessary conditions for frugality in eating and chewing thoroughly are fully met. The remaining residue from digestion will naturally decrease, avoiding severe discomfort in the internal organs. Stool volume will sharply decrease and will not emit a foul odor. The accumulation of feces in the intestines will be reduced. The nutrients from the food consumed will be fully utilized. Therefore, the overall condition will improve day by day. This is a natural principle. Therefore, my third recommendation to farmers is to eat less and chew more year-round, which can save a significant amount of money.

Farmers should seek hygiene practices that are both economical and cost-free. The economical methods have already been mentioned above. The cost-free methods, such as deep breathing and sunbathing, will be discussed further below.

Deep breathing is a kind of exercise that transforms the body and mind. It has three major benefits. It can provide the lungs with appropriate exercise, fully exchange air during breathing, enhance the lungs' resistance, and maintain the lungs' permanent health or eliminate existing lung diseases, especially tuberculosis in the apex of the lungs, which can be eradicated, making it the greatest effect of deep breathing, one. It can improve blood circulation in the brain. During deep inhalation, the pressure inside the chest cavity decreases, causing blood from the brain substance to flow downward. During exhalation, the pressure inside the chest cavity increases, causing the downward-flowing blood to flow back. This action can prevent all cerebrovascular diseases (such as cerebral hemorrhage, commonly known as stroke, which causes the most rapid death), two. It can improve blood circulation in the abdominal cavity. During deep inhalation, the pressure exerted on the surface of the stomach, intestines, liver, spleen, kidneys, etc., by the abdominal wall causes blood in these areas to flow in all directions. During exhalation, the pressure is released, and the blood flows back from all directions. This action can improve blood circulation in the abdominal cavity. The nerves distributed in the abdomen are also strengthened by the same action. Therefore, the function of the internal organs in the abdomen is enhanced, and various diseases cannot arise, three. In summary, deep breathing is nothing less than an invisible Great Wall for our lifeline. The air we breathe fills the heavens and earth, is free of charge, and is inexhaustible. It is also something that everyone can enjoy.

Hygiene experts in various countries around the world have different methods for performing deep breathing. Based on my personal experience, alternating breathing through the nostrils is the most suitable. The method is to stand in an open space outside, exhale the air from the lungs through both nostrils, exhaling as much as possible. Then, use one finger to press one nostril closed and inhale through the other nostril as much as possible. Then, release the finger and slowly exhale. This is one repetition. After each repetition, walk sixty steps, stand still, and then perform the second repetition. Perform about twenty repetitions each time, walking a total of one thousand two hundred steps. This can be timed or considered as a full-body exercise. Perform this about four or five times a day to reap the various benefits of deep breathing. This alternating nostril breathing method involves deep and powerful inhalation, which has appropriate effects on the various functions mentioned above. Furthermore, because the inhalation through one nostril is relatively gentle, the pressure in the chest cavity does not decrease abruptly, and the blood in the brain substance can flow down to the chest cavity gradually, preventing the brain from experiencing a sudden state of anemia and causing dizziness.

A Visit to the Sino-French Pharmaceutical Factory 151

— Chen Changhua

I have long admired the Sino-French Pharmaceutical Factory, as it has established a reputation throughout the country in just a few years. It must have remarkable achievements. I heard from a friend that the factory is one of the leading pharmaceutical factories in Shanghai. Its scale is rarely matched by other domestic companies in the industry. Recently, through a friend's introduction, I met Mr. Zhou Mengbai, the factory director, who is approachable and kind, and also one of the compilers of the Chinese Pharmacopoeia. His works can often be seen in various domestic medical and pharmaceutical journals. He is a pharmaceutical expert. He kindly invited me to visit the factory the next morning. Therefore, my friend and I were able to go on time, fulfilling my long-cherished wish of many years. How delightful!

The factory is located west of the Great Western Road in the city, covering an area of more than ten acres. The front of the factory buildings is a two-story Chinese-style building. The director's office and the general affairs department are located there. Workers eat and live there, and some of the factory's products are also stored there. (It is said that most of them are transported daily by the factory's own trucks to the main store, and then shipped to various places.) Further inside is a new-style three-story Western-style building made of steel and reinforced concrete. It is where the essence of the entire factory is concentrated. Most of the ground floor is used as a machine workshop, with seven or eight rooms. I will describe them separately below.

1. In the pill-making room, there are twelve pill-making machines. Each machine can produce about forty catties per day. There are also two powder-mixing machines, which are dedicated to mixing powders for pill-making. The machines are powered by motors, and the raw materials for the pills are purely Chinese medicine. The Lung Hu Brand Rendan, which we often take, and the newly advertised Xin Hong Dan, Lao Hong Dan, and Yin Dan, are all made there.

2. In the polishing room, there are four polishing machines. This is the final step in the production of Rendan. It is said that the cinnabar used for the coating of the Rendan is Guangdong cinnabar, so its luster is different from that of those who use Japanese cinnabar. This shows the factory's determination to use domestic products.

3. In the tablet-making room, there are two tablet-making machines, which are dedicated to making various tablets, such as Aspirin tablets, Cascara tablets, Happy Baby tablets, and Quinine tablets, totaling dozens of types. When we visited, the machine was pressing Luo Wei Aspirin tablets, which were accurately dosed and beautifully white, no wonder everyone likes to use them.

4. In the powder-making room, there are four powder-making machines, which are dedicated to grinding various powders, such as licorice, rhubarb, cinnamon, and cloves. The factory makes all powdered medicines itself. One of them is a Caites Integrator, which is also driven by a motor. It can compress large pieces into small pieces and crush coarse powder into fine powder, producing very quickly. The factory is also adding more powder-making machines because the current ones are insufficient, so the future output will be even more impressive.

5. In the drying room, there is a vacuum drying machine, which is very large. Next to it is a new-style air pump, and there are iron pipes to connect them. It is said that all medicines that cannot be dried with high heat can be dried in this machine. Next to the machine is another room with steam pipes, which uses the residual heat from the steam to dry various medicines. The room is also equipped with a temperature regulator and an electric fan, which can be said to be fully equipped.

6. In the sugar-coating room, there are two sugar-coating machines. The machines are round and have a warm exterior. There are fans on the side to regulate the heat and the evaporation of moisture. It is said that the accurately-dosed Elephant Brand sugar-coated Quinine tablets currently on the market are made there.

7. In the bottle-washing room, because the factory produces too many types of products, and the bottles are of different shapes and sizes, this washing work does not use machines, but uses manual labor. In addition to various washing devices, the room also has a steam drying oven and a steam disinfection oven. The bottles must be disinfected and dried after washing before they can be used. I always knew that the bottle-washing area was the most difficult to keep clean. Now that the factory pays attention to this, it is truly commendable.

In addition, there are also box-dressing rooms and powder-mixing rooms, etc. I was unable to observe them in detail, so I cannot describe them fully here. I will only note their names.

On the second floor is the manufacturing department, headed by pharmacist Lin Hongzao. All manufacturing matters in the factory are managed by this department, which includes the raw material stock, warehouse, formulation, and packaging sections. There is also a research laboratory for inspection or research purposes. That day, we saw that a medicine was being tested in the laboratory to see if it complied with pharmacopoeia regulations. Mr. Zhou said that recently, due to price competition, drug dealers often disregard ethics and engage in counterfeiting. Even a certain foreign-owned pharmacy on Nanjing Road has been found to be counterfeiting, which is regrettable. In terms of manufacturing, we saw the preparation of Ai Luo Brain Tonic, 914 Ointment, and other large quantities of medicines. These are handled in separate rooms to specialize in their respective tasks, as described below.

8. In the decoction room, there are two boiling machines, one pressure steaming machine, one heating and mixing machine, and one cold mixing machine. Brain tonic is made here. It is said that the work is busiest between autumn and winter, because in addition to brain tonic, Luo Wei Malt Extract Cod Liver Oil and Baby Cream must also be produced in large quantities to meet market demand.

9. In the distillation room, there are three distillation machines, one of which is dedicated to producing large quantities of distilled water. All water used in the factory for formulation is this water. The water is also supplied to the chemistry laboratories of several universities, such as Guanghua and Fudan, because it is pure and inexpensive. When we visited, we saw that one of the machines was distilling almond water. I know that most almond water on the market is made simply by adding almond oil to water, but this factory is able to manufacture it according to regulations, which is truly commendable.

10. In the maceration room, there are more than ten of the latest percolation devices and several pressing filters. All extracts, fluid extracts, and tinctures, etc., in the Chinese Pharmacopoeia and other national pharmacopoeias are manufactured here. It is said that the filters are very sophisticated, as they can quickly filter large quantities of products and filter substances that cannot be filtered by ordinary methods. For example, the factory's Emergency Epidemic Water is filtered using this machine, and it is said that the daily filtration volume can reach more than four thousand pounds.

11. In the oil-making room, various ointments are manufactured. The aforementioned 914 Ointment is made here. It is said that an average of one thousand dozen can be produced.

12. In the capsule room, various soft capsules are made, such as cod liver oil. When we visited, they were making 914 white cloudy medicine. Although there are many white cloudy medicines on the market, most of them are probably imported products repackaged or inferior goods disguised as the real thing. Now that the factory can manufacture it itself, it is truly admirable. It is also said that the formula is prepared according to the latest theories, so it has only been on the market for less than two years, and it has already been sold throughout the country, recovering rights and interests, not a small amount.

The above are all related to the formulation aspect.

Above, most of the space is used for paper box storage, and a small part is used for packaging. This room is dedicated to the packaging of large quantities of medicines. There are about sixty female workers, and their work is very efficient. To the left of the Western-style building is a row of Western-style buildings. The packaging section is also located on the upper floor. All individual items are placed there for packaging. The number of female workers is similar to that on the third floor. The ground floor is used to store raw materials. There is also a boiler room, located on the right side of the Western-style building. The boiler is not very large. It is said that it burns at most one ton of coal per day, but this is because the factory's power is purely electric, and the boiler's steam is only used for heating.

In addition, there is an eastern factory, which was newly expanded last year due to insufficient factory space. There is a row of flat tin buildings, covering an area of more than one acre, which serves as a warehouse for storing various glass bottles. There are also sixteen newly built flat rooms, including a mosquito coil manufacturing area, a pill-selection room, an ash-drying room, and a Rendan packaging room. It is said that the raw materials for manufacturing mosquito coils in the factory are also purely domestic products, such as pyrethrum, which are currently collected from Wuxi, Nantong, and other places. It is said that if domestic raw materials are not available, they would rather temporarily stop production. There are more than eighty female workers in the Rendan packaging room. This room can produce more than one hundred thousand five-fen packs of Rendan every day and night. It is said that this domestic Rendan was not originally manufactured there. Since Mr. Zhou took over, he has made significant improvements, so the recent products have improved a lot compared to before. It is believed that the people will definitely support it.

Overall, all parts of the factory are well-organized and have a thriving atmosphere. Although many foreign patent medicines are flooding the country, the factory only resists one-tenth of them. However, since the publication of the Chinese Pharmacopoeia, because Mr. Zhou is involved in the compilation of the Pharmacopoeia, the pharmacopoeial preparations he manufactures are all made according to the Chinese Pharmacopoeia, taking the lead in advocating their use. The raw materials also often undergo small-scale trials, which are all sufficient to show Mr. Zhou's efforts to develop China's pharmaceutical industry, not only to resist foreign goods but also to contribute to the people's livelihood. To save the country through industry, I have high hopes for Mr. Zhou.

Jiangsu Province Secondary School Entrance Examination Starts on the 21st of This Month 152

Publication of Experimental Methods

Examination Hall Rules

Examination Times for Each Subject

The Jiangsu Secondary School Graduation Entrance Examination Committee held a meeting at 3:00 PM on the 2nd at the Department of Education. More than 20 committee members including Shi Naikang and Chen Tianou attended. The meeting was chaired by Department Head Zhou. He reported that the purpose of holding the entrance examination was to comply with national policies on the one hand, and to consider the difficulties of young people on the other. After considering both aspects, a decision was made on the entrance examination guidelines. The selection of committee members was based on academic qualifications, economic status, and reputation, and they were selected from various schools in the province, but they did not represent any one school, but represented the entire education community of the province. It was hoped that all committee members would maintain a detached attitude and conduct a fair review. The meeting then resolved many examination matters, including the experimental methods. For example, Party Principles, Chinese Language, History, Mathematics, Physics, Chemistry, and Biology all used answers. English, Geography, and Testing used both testing and answers. Chinese Language had one essay question. English had one essay question, two question-and-answer questions, and ten sentence questions. Geography had ten testing questions and two essay questions. For other subjects, select four questions to answer. No additional questions may be answered beyond the specified question types for each subject. All examination questions will be written in classical Chinese, but scientific names should be noted with their original Western names. In addition, examination hall rules and examination timetables were also separately established. The following is an excerpt for the information of candidates.

Examination Hall Rules 153

1. Candidates should enter the examination hall according to the specified time for verification and take their seats according to the number assigned on the examination paper. No unauthorized changes are allowed.

2. Candidates should not bring any paper or notes other than the necessary stationery.

3. If a candidate commits any of the following, their examination paper will be invalidated:

(1) Engaging in or being the recipient of cheating.

(2) Bringing books or manuscripts.

4. If a candidate commits any of the following, points will be deducted:

(1) Talking and laughing with each other.

(2) Engaging in communication or passing of materials.

(3) Leaving one's seat without permission.

5. If a candidate commits any of the following, they will be immediately disqualified from the examination:

(1) Disrupting the order of the examination hall.

(2) Impersonating another candidate.

Disqualification is limited to one subject, but if discovered more than twice, the candidate will not be allowed to participate in the examination in that session.

6. Candidates should follow the instructions of the chief examiner and proctors.

7. Candidates should not ask the chief examiner or proctors about the meaning of questions or words.

8. Party Principles, National Language, History, and Geography should be written in brush. English, Mathematics, Physics, Chemistry, and Biology should be written in pen. All writing should be neat and clear.

9. Scratch paper is provided at the end of the paper. No separate paper should be used for drafting. Scratch paper and test papers must be submitted together with the examination paper.

10. Papers should be submitted within the prescribed time limit.

11. The floating signature on the examination paper should be verified by the proctor and removed on the spot. Candidates are not allowed to remove it themselves.

12. After submitting the paper, no requests for additions or alterations to words or sentences will be entertained.

13. After submitting the paper, candidates should immediately leave the examination hall and not return.

Beijing Prepares for Entrance Examination 155

Suzhou Elementary School Joint Association Opposes Elementary School Entrance Examination

The Ministry of Education has repeatedly issued orders for graduation entrance examinations for primary and secondary schools, which are bound to be implemented. However, the previous time, the Hunan Department of Education, due to special local circumstances, submitted a report to the Ministry of Education for some flexibility. Although the Ministry of Education stated that the matter was a misunderstanding of rumors, middle school students in various places have requested exemptions from examinations, and the Department of Education has had many difficulties in dealing with them. The Ministry of Education has requested instructions on how to proceed. The Ministry of Education replied to Fujian and other provinces yesterday that the middle school entrance examination is bound to be implemented, and it is hoped that the previous orders will be followed.

Private secondary school principals in Nanjing have repeatedly appealed for the entrance examination. The Nanjing Municipal Social Affairs Bureau has stipulated methods for holding the examinations in different districts. Although students want to be exempt from examinations, it is difficult to graduate without an entrance examination and there is nowhere to go for further education. In the end, they must take the examination.

However, the Beijing City area is actively conducting elementary school entrance examinations. The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau has notified various municipal schools to report the number of students graduating in the current year. It is said that some schools first consider the students' level and select the best ones to report (for example, if there are 30 sixth-grade students who are supposed to graduate this year, those with low abilities will be excluded, because the entrance examination has many failures, which are considered to be a standard for assessing the principal's performance. Therefore, everyone is in danger of losing their jobs and must plan ahead). On the one hand, teaching is being stepped up (some schools have temporarily revised their regular schedules for sixth-grade students, requiring them to come early and leave late, and even to attend school on Sundays). Subjects have been changed (some schools only teach Chinese, Arithmetic, and Social Studies to sixth-grade students every day, and no other subjects). As a result, teachers are overworked and students suffer (elementary school students' bodies are not fully developed, and their homework is increased in vain, and dreaming of the entrance examination every day is harmful to their health). This is definitely not good for the future of elementary school education. The graduating students of each school are reporting fewer students, which inevitably leads to family blame for those who have not graduated. To avoid questioning, the graduation examination problems held earlier in the school raise the standard, so as to avoid excuses. This matter is indeed an important issue for elementary schools, and it is not known how it will turn out.

The Jiangsu Provincial Experimental Elementary School Federation issued a declaration yesterday opposing the elementary school entrance examination, stating that holding graduation entrance examinations for elementary schools hinders the physical and mental development of children and is not in line with educational principles, arousing sympathy from the educational community.

Nanjing Women's Middle School Principal Tao Resigns 156

Qian Yonghe and Others Most Hopeful to Succeed

Tao Xuan, the principal of Jiangsu Provincial Nanjing Women's Middle School, is also a member of the Legislative Yuan. Tao has decided to resign as principal of the Women's Middle School to focus on her work as a member of the Legislative Yuan, as it is too strenuous to handle both positions. It is heard that the most hopeful candidates to succeed her are Qian Yonghe, Ni Liang, and Zhu Guangyu, all of whom have served as principals of the Xuzhou Women's Normal School (Qian, Ni, and Zhu have all served as principals of the Third Women's Normal School in Xuzhou).

Yang Lian, the new head of the Anhui Department of Education, took office on May 30th. There was a change in the staff of the department immediately. Wu Junsheng, Jin Yuan, and Wu Yifeng were newly appointed as secretaries. Zheng Hechun continues to serve as the head of the First Section. Zhang Xinpei, the original head of the Second Section, was transferred to Inspector. Zhang Dengshou, the head of the chief section, is acting as the head of the Second Section. Zhang Zhengping, the head of the Third Section and Inspector, is awaiting other appointments, and Xu Ningsheng, the chief clerk, is acting as the head of the Third Section. In addition, the staff of the Inspector Section and other officials can be fully announced within one or two days.

This City's Boy Scout Troop Held a Welcome Ceremony Yesterday for the Overseas Chinese Boy Scout Association from Fiji 159

More Than Thirty Boy Scout Troops and Over a Thousand Service Members

The Chinese Boy Scout Travel Group from Fiji has arrived in Shanghai for several days. The Shanghai Boy Scout Council, to foster friendship with the overseas Fijian Boy Scout group, specially convened all city boy scout troops to hold a welcoming ceremony yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM inside Shanghai High School on Shangwen Road. Approximately one thousand Boy Scouts and service members from more than thirty troops in this city attended, including Chengzhong, Anglo-American, Junyi, Shanghai High School, Jishi Elementary School, Yousheng, Jiangnan, Yucai, Dongya, Liangjiang, YMCA, Southeast, Guangdong, Guangyi, Wuyu, Yangjing, Minli, Lisheng, Linyin, Zhongguang, Fudan, Datong, Yangzheng, Dazhong, etc.

Chairman Zhao Weizu commenced the meeting as scheduled. First, the Chairman reported on the purpose of the welcome, followed by a speech by Wu Zongmu, leader of the Fijian Overseas Chinese Boy Scout Group, who stated that during this time of national crisis, our Boy Scouts should unite and work together to save the nation. He also detailed the pain of overseas Chinese regarding the weakening of China's international position. After the speech, variety show performances began, totaling more than thirty types, with the music and comedic dances of the overseas Chinese Boy Scouts being particularly outstanding. At 6:00 PM, refreshments were served, and the event concluded joyfully. On the spot, the Southeast, Jiangnan, and Lisheng troops presented the travel group with silver shields, Chengzhong presented a brocade banner, and Shanghai High School and Minli each presented a mirror stand as souvenirs. It is reported that the group is specially commissioned by the Central Propaganda Committee to film a lifestyle movie at the Lianhua Film Company today.

The University Faculty Association Issues a Declaration on Major Plans for National Salvation 160

The Shanghai University Faculty Association previously resolved at its sixth plenary executive committee meeting to issue a declaration on fundamental plans for national salvation. The declaration was drafted by the association's documentation section and reviewed and approved by Chairman Zhang Shouyong and others. The declaration stated that the root of China's illness lies in culture, and the remedy for revival is scholarship. Without culture, there is no way to recover; without scholarship, there is no way to save the country, and so on.

Hujiang University Calligraphy Society Invites Ma Gongyu to Give a Lecture 161

The Hujiang University Calligraphy Research Society recently invited calligrapher Ma Gongyu to give a lecture. Mr. Ma shared his more than thirty years of experience in studying calligraphy, explaining in detail the methods of holding the brush, using the brush, the steps of copying inscriptions, and the insights of calligraphers throughout history. The lecture lasted two hours, and the audience was packed.

The Wan Guo (International) Games Close in Drizzling Rain; The Championship Returns to China 162

China scores ninety-seven points; the United States is second with fifty-three points.

England is third, Russia fourth, Japan fifth, and Germany and France sixth.

The United States Sweeps the Women's Championship.

The Chinese Team Also Sets a New National Record in the 1600-Meter Relay.

The fourth Shanghai International Games closed yesterday in drizzling rain. The Chinese team won back the championship with 97 points. The United States was second with 53 points, England third with 30 points, Russia fourth, and Japan fifth. France and Germany followed. The women's championship for the second consecutive time was won by the United States, with their main athlete, Ms. Bennett, sweeping all the events, with amazing results. The Chinese women's team was only one point behind England, scoring sixteen to seventeen. Russia did not score any points. A total of six records were broken at the Games. Our relay team set a new national record in the 1600-meter relay with a time of 3 minutes and 41 seconds. Yesterday, the staff and athletes braved the rain, looking like drowned chickens, but their spirit remained unchanged, and the new record was the only consolation. Mrs. Tan Zhisheng presented the awards at the closing ceremony.

Our Athletes Set Two National Relay Records 165

In addition to Wang Jihuai setting a new Games record in the long jump (the previous highest Games record of 6.49 meters was also set by Mr. Wang, and now he has broken his own record with 6.705 meters), our Chinese athletes also set new national records in the 400-meter and 1600-meter relays, which is the greatest achievement for our athletes. It is noted that the previous highest national record for the 400-meter relay was 46.6 seconds, set by the Beijing team at the 15th North China Games in Jinan in 1931. Now, Huang Feilong, Dong Yinchu, Wang Jihuai, and Cheng Jinguan have broken it with 46 seconds. The previous highest national record for the 1600-meter relay was 3 minutes and 41.4 seconds, also set by the Liaoning team at the 15th North China Games in Jinan. Now, Zeng Rongzhong, He Debao, Dong Shuzhao, and Guan Changfa have broken it with 3 minutes and 41 seconds. However, although new national records were set, they did not break the Games records. The comparison is as follows:

400-Meter Relay 1600-Meter Relay

Our Original Record 46.6 seconds 3 minutes 41.4 seconds

New Record This Time 46 seconds 3 minutes 41 seconds

Games Record 44.8 seconds 3 minutes 38.6 seconds

Overview of Field Events 167

(1) Shot Put

Mironov's last push turned the tide. The preliminary three throws were almost dominated by the Chinese, occupying the top three positions. Gong Wanyu led with 12.13 meters, Leng Peigen was second with 11.89 meters, and Chen Baoqiu was third with 11.72 meters. Then came the Englishman McFee and Parker. The defending champion, Mironov, was in between McFee and Parker, ranking fifth with a score of 11.44 meters. It was thought that there would be no surprises. Who knew that Mironov's final sixth throw would be extraordinary, improving by more than one meter, allowing him to suddenly surge ahead? The results are as follows:

First: Motovkin (Russia) 12.44 meters

Second: Gong Wanyu (China) 12.13 meters

Third: Leng Peigen (China) 11.895 meters

Fourth: Chen Baoqiu (China) 11.795 meters

Fifth: McFee (England) 11.52 meters

Sixth: Parker (Germany) 11.33 meters

(2) Pole Vault

Chen Ling struggles to defeat his opponents. Yesterday's pole vault took more than two hours, a real hard battle. At first, it was thought that the Japanese might have good athletes, but unexpectedly, Hirato was eliminated after three jumps. Veteran Schwanck was fourth, and Chu Yinghuang was eliminated in third place with 3.26 meters. Chen Ling and Cao Yu fought hard, making it difficult to separate them. They both cleared 3.335 meters and then both fell. After adding back and forth, they went back to 3.26 meters. Both cleared it again and then fell. At this point, the two were exhausted. Cao fell, and Chen Ling was victorious. It can be called a hard-won battle.

First: Chen Ling 3.335 meters

Second: Cao Yu 3.335 meters

Third: Chu Yinghuang 3.26 meters

Fourth: Schwanck Unmeasured

(3) Javelin Throw

Hertson's specialty. There were many good athletes in the javelin throw, but the American was definitely going to be first. Wang Jihuai abandoned his attempt after knowing his thoughts were in vain after one throw. Hertson's first throw was 45.47 meters, securely taking the lead. The results of the four athletes are as follows:

First: Hertson (USA) 45.47 meters

Second: Mower (USA) 41.95 meters

Third: Yang Fang (China) 40.30 meters

Fourth: Mironov (Russia) 39.76 meters

(4) Triple Jump

Komatsu retains the championship. Last year's champion, Komatsu from Japan, broke his own record of 13.245 meters with 13.35 meters, retaining the championship. His last jump was powerful and impressive, truly a family tradition. A small red flag measured the steps accurately. The second was also a Japanese athlete. Our Wang Yongmin and He Zuxi were third and fourth. The results of the four athletes are as follows:

First: Komatsu (Japan) 13.35 meters (New)

Second: Oka (Japan) 13.295 meters (New)

Third: Wang Yongmin (China) 13.06 meters

Fourth: He Zuxi (China) 13.04 meters

(5) Women's Javelin

Bennett shines again. There were only five participants, three of whom were Chinese women, one being the beautiful Ms. Bennett and one being the Englishwoman Thompson. Thompson had not practiced this event and only managed a few meters. Two of her javelins were broken. Bennett could run and jump, but who knew she could also throw the javelin? When throwing the javelin, she had great momentum. The javelin flew like an arrow. Her first throw was 26.285 meters, not only setting a new Games record but also breaking the Chinese record of 24.20 meters. Chen Rongming was second with 23.63 meters, which was satisfactory. The results are as follows:

First: Bennett (USA) 26.285 meters

Racing Decisive Battle Record 170

(1) 100 Meters Yellash's Victory Not Easy

The first event of the finals in the drizzling rain was the men's 100 meters. With six people of equal strength, a fierce battle was expected. After the start, Cheng Jinguan took the lead, Tang Sly refused to be outdone, and the short Dongyang (Oka) tried his best to catch up. Yellash was in fourth place. In an instant, with only 30 meters remaining, Yellash chased hard with flying strides and full of vigor. At the finish line, Yellash had chased to the front and won by a shoulder. It was also quite dangerous. Time: 11.4 seconds. Cheng was second, Tang third, and Oka fourth. Huang Feilong and Monahan were eliminated.

(2) Women's 50 Meters Has Fierce Battle

American Thompson's women's ten are the highest record holders with seven seconds.

In the preliminary round, Ms. Bennett overwhelmed her. Yesterday's final was intended to avenge the previous hatred, but things went against her. Although she fought fiercely, she lost to Bennett again by one meter. The time was 7.2 seconds. Qian Xingsu tried hard to catch up and won third place, which was also gratifying.

(3) High Hurdles Chen Ling Suffers Miserable Defeat

Contrary to general expectations, the veteran Chen Ling could have won the championship, but unexpectedly, he encountered an opponent. In the first five hurdles, Chen Ling's strides were relaxed and extremely smooth. The little mustache Parker followed closely behind him without any reluctance. After the first five hurdles, the two were running shoulder to shoulder, holding on without giving way. The steps were even and the posture was beautiful. Even at the last hurdle, they were still on the balance line, but when Parker landed after clearing the hurdle, he took the lead and won the championship. Chen Ling's foot strength weakened slightly, leading to the lag, but they were only half a step apart. The time was 17.1 seconds, an improvement over the preliminary round. Guo Zhixin was third, and Mironov was fourth.

(4) Women's 100 Meters Still Belongs to Bennett

The situation in the women's 100-meter final was similar to that of the 50 meters. Thompson was again one meter behind and finished second. Ms. Bennett won another championship. The time was 13.5 seconds. The American Bauer was third, and Qian Xingsu勉强managed to get fourth place.

Med Hurdles First Tao Yingjie (Photo by Xu Tianzhang)

(5) Four People Compete in the 400 Meters

There were four Chinese in the 400-meter final, but before the race, Unknown Changfa and He De gave up the race. Only Sheppard, Zeng Rongzhong, Dengler, and Liu Fukang competed. It is said that Mr. Zheng will take a plane back to the troops to preside over the corps' affairs after the official matters are properly handled.

Spring and Autumn

The Northern Journey 174

— Huoxueming

Several years ago, I also took the Pingpu Railway train to visit the northern metropolis. Although yellow dust flew even during the day, filling my nose, this is my home, my motherland, I love it, I love it deeply, a nostalgic impression that is still very clear in my mind.

When the Japanese army's cannons broke through Shanhaiguan, the Blue Sky White Sun flag outside Shanhaiguan was buried; when the Japanese army's stray bullets from airplanes broke the Great Wall, the Manchurian flag with the yellow dragon and red sun replaced it outside the Great Wall; needless to say, if I have the opportunity to go north again, I want to go to Liaoning, Jilin, Rehe, Heilongjiang to see the vast forests, the towering snow mountains, and the vast ice rivers. Can I not obtain a travel permit from a certain country and say that I am going abroad?

I remember that during the period when a part of the National Army was fighting with the barbaric nation inside and outside the Great Wall, many young people went north to kill the enemy, followed by members of the Red Cross, who went north to rescue the wounded, followed by young ladies who brought biscuits and cigarettes to comfort the troops. Also, a large number of broadswords were manufactured and transported north to supply the enemy-killing efforts. During the period from September 18th to the recent armistice, in fact, there were also Central Army troops going north, Minister Song going north, Minister He going north, and even Chairman Chiang going north. Most recently, there was Chairman Huang Fu going north. Of course, we don't include those in the rear who, from some military and civilian organizations, sent telegrams saying they were going north, but were slow to act.

After all, Chairman Huang Fu's northern journey revealed a glimmer of hope for peace! We cannot but express our admiration and gratitude for the loftiness of this northern journey and the efforts to win honor for the country after going north. As for myself, living peacefully in Shanghai, writing Chinese characters, reading Chinese newspapers, and being considered a Chinese citizen on the household register, what reason do I have not to salute the angel of peace!

Even though I still have many brothers and sisters drifting in Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, Rehe; no, they are drifting abroad, they have not given me any news so far, perhaps they have been killed?

However, history tells us that a nation that does not resist deserves to be killed. From this point of view, what is there to complain about? Although, even though, perhaps, as a result of Chairman Huang Fu's efforts to negotiate under the four non-conditions (no loss of sovereignty, no humiliation of the country, no surrender, no compromise), the barbaric nation will return our lost territories, and at that time, the Blue Sky White Sun flag will once again fly over the forests, the snow mountains, and the ice rivers; then my compatriots who are now detained abroad will be returned to the Republic of China to be citizens! Needless to say: if we really have the opportunity to go north to see the ruins of the battlefield, we will neither have the trouble of obtaining a travel permit from a certain country, nor will we have the strength to say such a beautiful name: "Going abroad"?

Inconceivable 175

— Baihe

Mythical novels have become a distorted gift for Chinese children, so bank apprentices go to Mount Emei to seek immortals without saying goodbye, and 14-year-old elementary school students abandon their families and go to Wudang Mountain to visit Taoists. One scene after another is constantly being staged. After the national crisis began, the children's thoughts changed greatly, and they all hid at home, thinking about turning the gourd on the wall and the milk bottle on the table into magic treasures so as to scatter beans into soldiers and avenge the country. This is really a great success of Chinese education. One child suddenly saw a misty smoke outside the window, looking like auspicious clouds, and his heart suddenly blossomed. He jumped out of the window. But this child was not very skilled after all, and did not have the skills of Sun Wukong or Zhu Bajie. In the end, he could not jump out of the natural law of gravity and fell on a wonton stall under the building window. Although this is a joke, the inconceivable of Monk Jigong is still worshipped by everyone, who wishes to be Li Nezha or Tu Xingsun first.

I have a dear friend who observes his nose with his eyes and his mind with his nose, sits quietly, and after a long time, below the navel, above the perineum, between the small intestine and large intestine, outside the upper and lower dantian, in a part whose location is unknown to physiologists, he can generate a heat that can steam Shandong steamed buns, and he loses all consciousness and his yang energy flourishes. He feels comfortable all over. It is said that this heat, whose horsepower is unknown, is generated by the perverse flow of blood throughout the body, but it is definitely not a fever caused by fear of cold.

Wonderful, this is really the great way to prolong life and never grow old, which is more meaningful than Tai Chi and marathon, and more effective than the "Hundred-Year Machine". No wonder the straight-footed devils desperately worship the spiritual civilization of the mysterious Eastern country. Unfortunately, the current masses have incomplete Taoist bones and are not completely cleansed of the six senses. At the very least, they must go through ninety-nine and eighty-one tribulations before they can understand their own nature and become enlightened, achieve immortality and become a Buddha or ancestor, and ascend to heaven in broad daylight and become a world of immortals. It seems too early to talk about Tao in this 20th century.

Broken String 176

— Ye Yiyi

There are two major relatives in life: when you are young, at your maternal grandmother's house; when you are old, at your mother-in-law's house; and when you are old, at your son-in-law's house.

Money and women are equally important in this extremely sharp capitalist city. Money can buy women, and women can make money.

Money, vanity, and licentiousness are the characteristics of the city. But the children and wives of the gentlemen who advocate maintaining morality and combating extravagance are playing the leading roles in these characteristics.

Many young people, if they suddenly find that on any corner of a book, or a piece of news, or an advertisement, there are words about women, or kissing and hugging, or romance and affairs, they will always quietly read it.

Women are born with an instinct to seduce; their smiles, their eyes, and their voices are the tools of seduction!

Some people say that women are vases; but I say that's not right. Because there are countless hardworking women in China who live inhuman lives.

When an elderly widow sees her children in pairs, that is her happiest moment, and also her saddest moment!

Shaving Poem 177

— Qing Qu

Speaking of the word "shaving," it is also a tragic fact in history. In June of the second year of the Shunzhi period of the early Qing Dynasty, an edict was issued ordering the tonsure of hair. If anyone violated this edict, they would be "killed without mercy." Therefore, when the decree arrived in various counties, there was a severe penalty of "keep your head, not your hair; keep your hair, not your head." Even many shaving craftsmen were hired to carry the burden and parade in the streets. When they saw people with long hair, they would grab them and forcibly shave them. If they did not obey and resisted slightly, they would kill their heads and hang them on the poles of the burden to show the public. How cruel! Later, there were many people who died as martyrs because of this. There were even those who built "hair mounds" and secretly wept to offer sacrifices to express their sorrow. Therefore, the staunch defense of Jiangyin and the three massacres of our county can be said to have largely originated from shaving. The day before yesterday (the 29th of last month), I saw Mr. Huoxueming quoting a poem, "Hearing that the head can be shaved, now it is actually shaved." I remember that the old man from Deqing Dianqian also wrote an ancient meaning of shaving. This poem was not included when he compiled the poems, I don't know why, perhaps it was out of playful writing, then it was discarded. Just now I found the old manuscript I copied when I was a child in the pile of old paper, and I wrote it down. It can be seen that this old man depicted the matter of shaving more thoroughly.

Life is a matter of inches of skin, everything is sold, is it really a disease in the head, and then cut like grass, there are ancient sayings, quite enough for an examination, it seems to make it disappear, what is there with fleas, to compare the treatment of mountain bandits, first remove their way, who is this word for, so that Fubo old, try it on the little eunuch, and immediately will be sure to fall, after that Wen Tianxiang, there are poems in the posthumous manuscripts, hair is gone, the heart will exist, imagine the heat like a brazier, and I was born today, quite feel this thing is good, both to avoid the strong man rushing, also reduce the Shangshan Hao, after ten days without a shave, the head is like a pomelo, who is the executor of this, short clothes and broken jacket, into the kitchen call for soup, startled away the ginger-soup wife, pour water to wash the head basin, prostrate and salt the brain, a foot of cloth is not sewn, even more rough than the Lu gauze, to replace the grindstone, still able to protect the blade, but hear the sound of hoh, like cutting rice in the field, the bottom is carried by a plate, offering like a jade scepter, passing by the falling flowers, full head of defeated leaves swept away, I am not Tao Pengze, bending over also not annoyed, or even close both eyes, indistinguishable from white and black, lowering the head of millet and wheat, suddenly new as jujube, if there are louse-like ministers, do not ask the embryo or the aborted, after holding the hair three times, abandon the old and create a new one, interlaced green coral, black agate, my body leans for a long time, like wood branches withered, and you push and knock, like a bitter chanting island, the ear door does not allow wheat, also indulge in exploration, the tool is stored in a tube, should be called a gourd set, in a short while the skills are exhausted, and then wash the cheeks, looking at all kinds of hair, the wind is not dry, reward with bronze coins to the wine shop old woman, and I sit in a room, ears and eyes are washed from the heat, get up and look at the sunny sky, peep at the sun still bright, beard collection is not Northeastern Company Commander 178

Episode 8

Furious Words Arouse Youth, Who Resigns from Office and Flees

Enthusiastic Compassion for Young Woman, Who Brings Cotton for Warmth

The two of them talked in the room for a long time. Mrs. Gan, in the main room, vaguely heard a sentence or two, which surprised her very much.
