Ji smiled faintly: "There is no such thing as a conflict. He is the director, and I am a staff member. Logically, I should be reprimanded by him." Mrs. Gan said: "Why do you have to be so resolute? You can always talk things over slowly. If your brother is wrong, I can help you judge the matter when he comes back. If you are wrong, it doesn't matter if your brother says a few words to you. No matter how wronged you are, wait for your brother to come back and talk about it." Ji shook his head and smiled: "I don't want to see him. Seeing his face will only lead to another lecture. Why should I be so spineless?" As he spoke, he continued to pack things on the table. Mrs. Gan said: "If you really want to leave, we can't stop you. But I don't know what happened between you two brothers that caused the dispute. You should let your brother come back before you leave, so I can give him an explanation." Ji pulled a long face and said: "Sister-in-law, do you think I have done something improper and ran away behind my brother's back? If that's what you think, I'll wait here for two hours, wait for my brother to come back before leaving. But there is one thing, I am the one who is leaving, please tell my brother not to scold me anymore." (90)

Women's Paradise

Housewife's Must-Knows 179

— Chu

How to Preserve the Freshness of Vegetables

The types of vegetables we eat daily vary with the seasons. However, only people living in the countryside can eat fresh vegetables every day. As for those living in cities, they often cannot buy fresh goods on the same day due to uneven distribution and supply. Even if they can buy fresh goods on the same day, there are leftovers that are left for the next day, and there are also those who buy more ingredients in preparation for two or three days. Therefore, housewives should have a certain knowledge of preservation for the vegetables they buy every day, so that the vegetables they eat will not lose their fresh flavor. Now I will talk about the method of preserving freshness: First, after buying all kinds of green vegetables, they should be placed on dark sandy soil. It is most taboo to sprinkle water or soak them in water, and all kinds of vegetables must not be mixed, but should be stored separately. For example, taro and yam must not be placed in a humid place. If stored in this way, they will not lose their original fresh flavor. Ordinary women without common sense often do not know how to preserve them. Afraid that the vegetable leaves will dry out, they often sprinkle water on them or soak them in water. On the surface, they seem to be very fresh, but in fact, they not only lose their fresh flavor, but also the original chlorophyll, iron, and other nutrients are decomposed due to the water. Second, do not hang them in a ventilated place. If you are afraid that they will dry out, you can wrap them in two or three layers of newspaper. The outer newspaper should be sprayed wet with water and then tied tightly with a rope. Hang them in a dark place where there is no light, and they can be preserved for many days. As for the methods of preserving other types of vegetables, they vary according to their nature and shape. For example, melons, bamboo shoots, and eggplants, if they are to be preserved for seven or eight days, can be placed in a basket and filled with fir and cypress branches all around. If they are to be preserved for several months, you need a dry jar, with three or four parts of yellow sand paved below. Put the melons, bamboo shoots, eggplants, etc. on top, keeping each item from touching each other. Then fill it with two or three parts of yellow sand. After it is full, cover it tightly with thick straw paper, then dig a hole in the ground and put the jar in the hole, covering it with five inches of soil. Then, even after a year, it will not rot. Cabbage can be placed under dark sandy soil or wrapped in newspaper to preserve it for many days. However, when placing it, the cabbage heart should be facing upwards, and it must not be immersed in water, otherwise the cabbage heart will rot. However, the nature of celery is relatively different and should not be too dry. If you want to preserve its fresh flavor, you can wrap it in a damp towel and place it on a plate. Peas should be stored in a dark place with the pods attached, and they can be preserved for a long time. Fresh mushrooms should be filled with fir and cypress leaves and hung in a ventilated place. Ginger should be stored in a dry place away from sunlight, or it can be stored in a cement jar. In short, there are many types of vegetables, and it is impossible to explain them in detail one by one. It is best to place them on dark sandy soil away from sunlight, or to store them in a sandy soil jar. As for aristocratic families, they naturally have refrigerators and other various equipment, and even if they rot, they can be discarded at will. However, middle-class and lower-class families, in this era of expensive rice and firewood, buy vegetables with money earned from blood and sweat, and for economic reasons, they naturally cannot be discarded at will. However, everyone does not know how to preserve them, so they cannot store the leftovers for a long time and lose their fresh flavor, which is a great pity. As for fish and meat, you should distinguish their color. Beef and pork with bright red color are the best. The meat from the back and middle part of the animal is the most tender, that is, the part in the middle of the back bones and tendons. The meat from the buttocks is medium-grade meat, and the meat from the feet is low-grade meat. Low-grade meat is not easy to digest, and the nutrients are also relatively less. It is more difficult to choose fresh fish than other items. First, see if the scales of the fish are bright and if they do not easily fall off when you touch them with your hand. Second, smell the fish to see if its smell has changed. Third, see if the eyes of the fish are bright or sunken inward. Fourth, see if the color of the fish gills is bright red and transparent. Fifth, press the fish meat with your finger. If the finger leaves the fish meat and it is elastic and can still return to its original shape, it is fresh. If it is sunken and cannot recover, it is already rotten. Sixth, the anus of the fish is light red and protruding. Seventh, the fish belly is not easy to break. Eighth, the internal organs are not exposed. Ninth, if it is placed in water and sinks to the bottom, it is fresh. If it floats on the surface, it is rotten.

Page 17

Free Talk

"Showing Off" Defense 180

— Cao Juren

I have always mostly used my real name when writing articles, because I am easily moved by my personal experiences, and I cannot help but touch upon sensitive realities. I take responsibility for my own words to avoid implicating friends. I seek peace of mind and have no intention of "showing off" by doing this. I do not accept Mr. Yingying's claim that I am "showing off to a great extent."

Observing the world, what living beings enact is either tragedy or comedy. Even something like "love of showing off" may not always go as one wishes. Cao Kun rose from a small cloth merchant to a military inspector and then became the President. He had experienced the full range of worldly riches and could be said to have shown off to the fullest extent. In 1926, when Beijing was recruiting soldiers, some people used this as a front for their own purposes. At that time, there must have been many who dreamed of wearing a diagonally slung belt. Seeing this sign, they fully believed they could gain an official position to brag about to their neighbors. But some, like Wei Yancan, ended up drowning his wife and killing his children, then throwing himself into the Huangpu River; others, like a certain staff officer, couldn't even get a job pulling a rickshaw. They either earned pity or were ridiculed. Only then did they realize that it was all a mistake based on the idea of "wanting to show off." My friend N, in 1924, felt depressed and unfulfilled, and went to Guangdong, enrolling in the Whampoa Military Academy. In 1927, he returned to Zhejiang from Jiangxi in glory. How impressive! Many friends wanted to give up writing and join the army, going to Beijing to take the military academy entrance exam. I said, "Cao Kun came from selling cloth, that's true. But don't forget, Yuan Shikai trained troops at Xiaozhan."

"At that time, Cao Kun was already a platoon leader. From training troops at Xiaozhan to becoming the Minister of Beiyang, from the Minister of Beiyang to becoming the President of the Republic, the Xiaozhan buddies became the big shots of Beiyang. The development of this group should absolutely not be ignored. The ancients spoke of fate and opportunity, and opportunity is the most important. Waiting until Cao Kun became the President to 'stand at attention and rest' would be too late!" Sure enough, they wore the diagonally slung belts for three years and then went home to eat old rice. Starting with the desire to show off and ending with bad luck, you can still let me say, "Unfortunately, I was right," which is of course a type of comedy.

Then there are those who want to show off and actually do show off. Three or five years ago, a certain person flipped a somersault and became a popular figure in Shanghai, commanding a hundred responses with a single call, and having a house full of wives and concubines. Friends said that no one was more successful at showing off than this person. But before long, he flipped another somersault and became a nobody. His door was deserted, and no one paid attention to him. Suffering when gaining and suffering when losing, Mencius became a prophet from thousands of years ago. Because they could "be arrogant to their wives and concubines" and "many poor people could get help from me," many people unknowingly were forced onto the path of showing off. When embarking on this path, they would "bid farewell to the old flowers and willows of South Lake, to keep the misty moon company with the returning oars." Once they reached "the Eastern Market, the official robes were measured and ended, and the earth of Northern Mountain could not be kept," they could only say "Too late to regret." Even if they show off, they still cannot avoid acting out a tragicomedy, so what is there to say? As for criticizing figures, there has never been a good outcome in ancient or modern times. Confucius, a master of praise and criticism, lived a restless life, running into walls everywhere. Kong Rong was outspoken, and Cao Cao simply sent him to the execution ground. Ruan Ji and Ji Kang, two masters of humor, even though they drank and took medicine every day, still offended the authorities, who said they were destroying the proper teachings. Truly, truly, the lesson of the Xia Dynasty is not far off. Recently, Ji Kang's family instructions taught his son to be careful in his dealings. One instruction said not to visit officials too often, nor to stay overnight. When officials see people off, do not be behind them, because it is feared that when officials punish bad people in the future, you will be suspected of secretly reporting them. Another instruction said that if there is an argument at a banquet, you should leave immediately to avoid criticizing from the sidelines, because there must be right and wrong between the two parties. Not criticizing is not proper, but criticizing will mean that one party will dislike the other. The old masters of pure conversation did not encourage their children to criticize figures. To want to show off by criticizing figures is the act of a fool.

The first chapter of the philosophy of showing off should be "Show off less." Lao Tzu's "guarding the feminine" and "guarding the black" mean this. If writing articles is for the sake of showing off, then I might as well put down my pen.

The Origin of Flower Gambling 181

— Li Tiao

I discussed flower gambling last time. In the article, I was quite critical of flower gambling. Yesterday, I came across Inoue Koubai's "Wine, Sparrow, and Opium," which had a chapter on the origin of flower gambling. After reading it carefully, I suddenly realized that I had been disrespectful to this beneficial business. I am now translating it to record my error.

"The origin of flower gambling is said to be as follows:

In the past, when the Luoyang Bridge in Henan had not yet been built, the people on both sides of the river found it very inconvenient and often prayed that someone would build a bridge there. The Jade Emperor was moved and summoned Guanyin Bodhisattva, ordering her to build the bridge. Guanyin Bodhisattva felt that it was very difficult without funding. After trying all sorts of methods, she had to use her own beauty, rowed a boat, and stopped on the side of the river, proclaiming that she would marry whoever could throw silver onto her body. She then transformed into twelve beautiful incarnations standing at the bow of the boat. The people on both sides of the river threw countless amounts of money at her, but no one could hit her. At that time, a beggar priest came. He took out a piece of silver from his dirty sock and threw it at Guanyin Bodhisattva. Not only did it hit, but it landed perfectly on Guanyin Bodhisattva's chest. Guanyin Bodhisattva was extremely surprised. Who was this beggar priest? She calculated with her fingers and realized that it was the Taoist patriarch Lü Dongbin. So Guanyin Bodhisattva said very angrily:

"I am doing this for the convenience of the people, and you are hindering me. Now I am leaving and you are responsible for everything!" After saying this, Guanyin Bodhisattva's form disappeared. Lü Dongbin, having caused trouble, thought carefully. Although this was annoying, he had to build the bridge as the Jade Emperor had ordered. So he thought and thought, and came up with the game of 'flower gambling.' Previously, gambling was one-to-one odds, but flower gambling paid thirty times the bet if you won. Therefore, men and women, young and old, all came to sell, and in an instant, a huge amount of money was raised and the bridge construction was completed."

After translating Inoue Koubai's wonderful article, I couldn't help but think that there are indeed many Guanyin Bodhisattvas and Lü Dongbins in China today. Look, aren't those embracing, compassionate Guanyin Bodhisattvas sacrificing their looks? Look, isn't it clearly written below that big kite: 52,000 yuan? The clever immortal Grandpa Lü Dongbin has innovated and come up with some deformed "flower gambling" games.

Guanyin Bodhisattva and Pure Yang Patriarch have all descended to the mortal world together, so how can China not become strong!

Faded Life 182

— Da Wu

As it was getting dark, there was a sudden commotion downstairs, with everyone talking at once, making it hard to hear. Xunzhen, who loves to watch the excitement, hurriedly dropped the unfinished clothes she was cutting and went downstairs. Downstairs, I only heard someone saying amidst the noise, "Goodness, luckily the weather is warm. Otherwise, he would have died of the cold even if he didn't drown."

Ten minutes later, Xunzhen came running upstairs with news. She started by saying, "Shen Tianxi, the man who sells chicken and duck blood downstairs, jumped into the Huangpu River."

Jumped into the Huangpu? I was shocked. Jumping into the Huangpu means seeking death, suicide. Why would he seek death? So I listened to Xunzhen's story. She said:

"He jumped in but was rescued by the water police. Just now the police came and called away the landlord and his niece, A Jin. It's still not known if he's alive or dead."

As long as he was rescued, he probably didn't die. Otherwise, how would the police know his home and come to notify them? In just three days, another big event happened in this building. Two days ago, the woman in the shanty gave birth. I heard the baby crying, then heard adults calling the woman's name, and soon heard the family wailing, saying she had died. In less than an hour, a life was born into this world and another life died. At the time, I thought that a living person had to exchange a life in order for a life to be safely preserved. Little did she know that people would use life to exchange for life.

Yet here was another life hovering on the edge of death. That woman gave birth to exchange for a life, so what was this for? From spring to summer, the newspapers report news of people throwing themselves into the Huangpu River every day. Probably this piece of news will be published in the newspaper tomorrow as well. Usually, news in the newspaper is labeled as "Unable to make a living..." Isn't it also that they seek death in order to seek life? Old Man Shen probably isn't an exception, right? But I became suspicious and started thinking irrationally:

Old Man Shen is a middle-aged man with a smiling face and a kind disposition, dark-skinned and tall with a full beard. Although we often do business with him, buying sixty or one hundred coins worth of fresh chicken and duck blood, we don't talk much. Sometimes when I come back late at night, Xunzhen doesn't dare to go downstairs, so he mostly opens the door for me. His bed is right in the downstairs living room. During the day, he puts away the mosquito net and leans the bed board against the corner of the wall. He doesn't have a wife, she died long ago. He has a niece who is fourteen or fifteen years old, who washes clothes and cooks at home. I heard that he raised her since she was little. He goes out to do business in the early morning and morning, and comes home in the afternoon. When doing business with him, I once asked him how much business he could do in a day, and he said that after deducting the capital, he could earn four or five strings of cash a day. We exclaimed that it was a good business. However, his clothes are tattered, patched upon patched. We assume that he is overly frugal, wanting to save money and rebuild his dream. Because he is at most forty years old. That's all I know. But he is seeking death today. I decided that it is not "unable to make a living," because he can earn four or five strings of cash a day.

Soon more news came from downstairs. What it was, I didn't know. I was lost in thought, smoking a cigarette in my fingers, trying to explore the cause of this suicide by drowning. Xunzhen sat next to me and said:

"Old Man Shen didn't die, he's in the hospital now. A Jin just came back. Yesterday was the Dragon Boat Festival. Old Man Shen went out yesterday. When he left, he asked A Jin to do his business for a day in his place, saying he had something to do in Pudong. He told her to keep the money from the sales carefully, and if she didn't see him come back, to pack up her things and go back to her hometown in Changzhou. Old Man Shen was preparing to seek death."

"Do you know why he sought death now?"

"According to the landlord, he owes too much usurious interest, and the money he earns isn't enough to pay the interest. He often said he wanted to seek death, or leave Shanghai. Yesterday, when he went out, A Jin thought he was running away from debt."

So that's how it is. Although Old Man Shen earns four or five strings of cash a day, he ultimately cannot escape the example of "unable to make a living." Yet now he can't even seek death. This life, there's really nothing that can be done with it.

The next day, Old Man Shen came back, still with his dark face and full beard, but the smile on his face was gone. When I saw him, I thought to myself, is he back from the edge of death? Yet he carried on with his business as usual. A Jin took out a silver dollar and told Xunzhen that this was the money he had with him that day when he left, and it hadn't been lost after being tossed around in the water. Shunzhen said that the character pasted on top made of cut red paper had faded in color. That was naturally because it had been soaked in water. Old Man Shen's heart, I thought, was probably somewhat like that red character. A little faded, right?

In less than a month since moving into this building, I have seen two sad things: one is exchanging a life for a life, and the other is washing a little color off a life in the water.

Carrot Hair 183

— JULES KENARD, translated by Lin Qu

The Sheep

Carrot Hair first only saw some blurry, moving spheres. These spheres emitted deafening, mixed cries, just like some children playing in the school's two playgrounds. The spheres hit against his crotch, making him feel a little uncomfortable. Another sphere was wriggling fiercely under the light from the small window in the roof. It was a lamb. Carrot Hair smiled because he had been startled. His eyes gradually adjusted to the darkness, and he could see the situation inside clearly. The lambing season had arrived. Every morning, the small tenant farmer Bazzole could add two or three lambs. He found them wandering among the ewes, looking dull-witted, their bodies standing on stiff legs, like four very thick pieces of wood, trembling.

Carrot Hair still didn't dare to touch them. But they were bolder, sucking on his shoes, or holding a piece of dry grass in their mouths, stepping on him with their front feet.

Those that were a week old powerfully stretched their bodies, twisting and turning in the air. Those that were only a day old were very weak, often kneeling down, but still standing up energetically. A lamb that had just been born was crawling on the ground, still sticky and not yet licked. Its mother, obstructed by a swaying bag full of water, pushed it away with her head. "This is a bad mother!" Carrot Hair said.

"It's the same in animals as it is in humans," Bazzole said.

"She must want to give it to a wet nurse."

"Almost like that," Bazzole said. "Some lambs have to be fed with a feeding bottle, like the kind we buy at the pharmacy."

Bottle, but it doesn't last long, because the mother will be moved. And we can also force the mother to give in."

He grabbed her shoulder and dragged her away, placing her in a bottle. He tied a grass collar around her neck, so she could be identified if she drowned. The lamb followed its mother. The ewe loudly ate grass, and the lamb weakly looked up, standing on its soft feet, looking for milk to eat, looking very pitiful, its face covered in a trembling, congealed juice.

"Do you think she will have a day when she becomes more compassionate?" Carrot Hair said?

"Yes, when her lower body is better," Bazzole said. "She was in a lot of pain when she gave birth."

"But I still think my idea is good," Carrot Hair said. "Why not temporarily give the lamb to another ewe to nurse?"

"She would refuse," Bazzole said.

Indeed, the cries of the ewes from the four corners of the sheepfold, announcing that it was feeding time, mixed together. The cries sounded monotonous to Carrot Hair's ears, but to the lambs, they had subtle differences, because each lamb jumped straight to its own mother's udder without any confusion.

"There are absolutely no ewes here that steal children."

"It's strange, this kind of family instinct in sheep," Carrot Hair said, "How can they distinguish the smell?" Maybe it's because"

Sense of smell is keen."

He almost wanted to plug a sheep's nose to test it.

He compared humans and lambs carefully, he wanted to know the names of the lambs. (To be continued)

Page 18

Economic Special Issue No. 25 Published on Mondays

How to Revive China's Silk Industry Shang Hoping 184

The reasons for the decline of China's silk industry, listed in the biggest, can be analyzed as follows:

Foreign (1) The world's economic downturn; (2) The exploitation by Japanese silk; (3) The partial squeezing out of artificial silk.

Domestic (1) Declining rural economy; (2) The use of scientific methods to improve mulberry trees, silkworm eggs, silk, etc. has not yet become widespread; (3) The political capabilities of the central and local governments are rarely used to fundamentally address and relieve the silkworm industry; (4) Transactions of silk, cocoons, silkworm eggs, mulberry, etc. completely lack appropriate organizations; (5) Sound central research silk authorities are still lacking."

In this complex environment, in order to seek effective countermeasures, can be divided into palliative and fundamental solutions, and progress simultaneously. Among the palliative measures, the reduction and exemption of taxes on silk cocoons, etc., and various incentives, have been gradually implemented by the Central Government and the provincial governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang, and will not be discussed in detail here. However, palliative and fundamental measures must be mutually reinforced, otherwise they will lose their effectiveness and cannot be sustained, and will inevitably be abandoned halfway. Now, the fundamental strategies are described in detail as follows:

My country's raw silk used to be sold to Europe and the United States, and in recent years the European and American markets have been completely seized by Japanese silk. There are three reasons for this: (1) The quality of raw silk is not pure; (2) There is too little silk of the same quality, which cannot meet the demand of the European and American markets; (3) The cost is too high, and it cannot compete with others' low prices. Moreover, these three problems are interrelated, so fundamental solutions must be resolved simultaneously. The solution can be divided into agriculture, industry, and commerce to achieve the goal of low prices, good quality, and large quantities.

A. In terms of agriculture:

The raw material of silk is cocoon. The quality and price of cocoon, whether it is pure or mixed, depends on whether scientific methods are applied to planting mulberry trees, making silkworm eggs, and raising silkworms, and whether there is an appropriate organization. Therefore, the following should be carried out simultaneously. (1) "Planting mulberry trees" actual situation; mulberry is the raw material of cocoon, so we must first seek its low price and good quality. According to recent years, in the prosperous areas of sericulture in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, the average yield of leaves per mu of mulberry field is less than seven or eight dan, compared with a reasonable mulberry garden, which can produce more than 20 dan per mu, only one-third of the production. If there are floods and insect pests, or farmers are poor and there is insufficient fertilization, the production is even lower, so the leaf quality is poor and the cost is heavy. (Improvement measures;) In areas where mulberry improvement has reached a considerable level, lend mulberry seedlings and fertilizers to farmers, and guide the new methods of deep plowing, cutting mulberry trees, and removing insects. (2) "Making silkworm eggs" (actual situation;) The achievements of improving silkworm eggs have been recognized by the society and farmers, so there is no need to discuss it, but the quantity is still small, the supply cannot meet the demand, and it cannot be popularized, which is regrettable. According to the three provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui, the annual demand for silkworm eggs in spring and autumn is about 12 million sheets, and the current output is less than 20%, among which there are still rough and shoddy products to make up the numbers, and the required 120,000 sheets of silkworm eggs have not completely specified the manufacturing agency. (Improvement measures;) Private egg farms should be supervised and encouraged by the government, and implemented at the same time. Select a suitable location, plant a large number of mulberry gardens for seed use, and recruit merchants to produce silkworm eggs to supplement the insufficient quantity of silkworm eggs. At the same time, the central government should set up an experimental farm for the research and unification of varieties, and stipulate the varieties used throughout the country. (3) "Raising silkworms" (actual situation;) In unimproved sericulture areas, farmers use local species. From raising the silkworms to going up to the cluster, everything does not conform to scientific methods, and the harvest is less than one-tenth or two-tenths. Even if the harvest is slightly abundant, the cocoon quality is also poor, so the silkworm raising method urgently needs guidance. (Improvement measures;) Set up a model area for improving sericulture, organize silkworm-raising cooperatives, so as to guide farmers' silkworm-raising methods, and set up guidance stations in places where there are no model areas. It can disinfect, raise silkworms and raise young silkworms on behalf of farmers, and guide them to improve the method of going up to the cluster. (4) "Improving the organization of cocoon collection" In addition to the above three items, the organization of cocoon collection also has a great relationship in improving cocoon quality. The organization of cocoon collection is not good, the evaluation is not commensurate with the cocoon quality, that is, there is no way to reward high quality, and the promotion of improvement will naturally be hindered invisibly. The varieties of raw material cocoons are mixed, the quality of silk produced is low, and the cost is increased. This is the biggest reason for the failure of silk mills in recent years. Therefore, we should use scientific management methods to improve the organization of cocoon collection. The evaluation should be suitable, so that we can collect high-quality cocoons at a high price, and eliminate inferior cocoons. We should also pay attention to the purity of varieties, which is an important key to improving cocoon quality in addition to the above three items.

B. In terms of industry;

The success or failure of silk mills is of course very important to the raw material cocoons, as mentioned above, but the precision of machinery and the legality of management are also important. Promote the establishment of new silk mills (multi-strand slow-speed silk machines) and improve old silk mills, in order to increase the output of high-grade raw silk (uniformity above 83 points), so as to compete with Japanese silk in the European and American markets, because Chinese silk of the same grade as Japanese silk is more popular in the European and American markets.

C. In terms of commerce;

My country's raw silk has no sound organization in international market trade. Each transports and sells, each acts on its own, and each does not plan for each other. There is no transport and sales agency at home and abroad to be responsible for investigation, promotion, and publicity. Compared with Japan, it is inevitable that it will be inferior. Therefore, the organization of international transport and sales agencies and the establishment of silk financial institutions to regulate them are all urgent measures.

To sum up the above, agriculture is planting mulberry trees, making silkworm eggs, raising silkworms, and selling cocoons; the silk industry is from agriculture, industry, and commerce. From beginning to end, vertical and horizontal mutual relations must have a consistent policy, and everything must have a connection organization, in order to achieve the most economical purpose. On the one hand, we should use the superior silk quality, low labor cost, and suitable soil and climate of our country, and at the same time use scientific new methods to proceed. If we can do so, and its products cannot compete in the international market and cannot restore its former glory, who can believe it?

Policies for Improving China's Silk Industry by Xia Dao Xiang 185

Raw silk is now an international trade commodity. The rise and fall of its exports can be used to measure the prosperity or decline of a country's silk industry. By looking at the table below, we can imagine the state of our country's silk industry in recent years.

Table of Chinese Silk Exports (Quantity unit: dan; Value unit: Customs taels)

Year | Export Quantity | Export Value

------- | -------- | --------

Republic of China Year 15 | 168,563 | 144,826,358

Republic of China Year 16 | 160,002 | 128,705,732

Republic of China Year 17 | 180,186 | 145,443,481

Republic of China Year 18 | 189,980 | 147,681,338

Republic of China Year 19 | 151,429 | 109,181,124

Republic of China Year 20 | 136,186 | 84,680,482

Republic of China Year 21 | 78,219 | 32,932,250

From the above table, we know that the export of raw silk from our country recently, whether in terms of quantity or value, has decreased sharply. However, compared with the figures of the United States, the largest consumer of raw silk in the world, and Japan, the largest exporter, listed in the table below, the difference is much greater. (The consumption of the United States and the export volume of Japan have not decreased, only the price has fallen.)

Table of Raw Silk Consumption in the United States and Raw Silk Exports in Japan

Year | Raw Silk Consumption in the United States (dan) | Raw Silk Export Volume in Japan (dan) | Value (Japanese Yen)

------- | -------- | -------- | --------

Republic of China Year 15 | 510,546 | 442,978,743 | 052,443

Republic of China Year 16 | 551,379 | 521,773,742 | 265,820

Republic of China Year 17 | 571,010 | 549,256,733 | 436,584

Republic of China Year 18 | 619,747 | 80,950,784,150 | 494

Republic of China Year 19 | 582,226 | 477,322,419 | 107,335

Republic of China Year 20 | 594,889 | 660,417,356 | 694,256

Republic of China Year 21 | 553,818 | 548,236,382 | 878,689

From this, we have two major questions: 1. The world's consumption of raw silk has not decreased, and Japan's exports remain the same. Why is our country's exports so small? 2. Our country is far superior to Japan in terms of the factors of silk industry operation. Why can Japan maintain its previous export volume even after repeated sharp declines in silk prices, while our country declines miserably after a slight blow and cannot recover? What is the reason? In my opinion, the authorities in charge of the Japanese silk industry have been striving to improve the quality of raw silk to meet the needs of Europe and the United States. At the same time, they have been working hard to reduce the cost of raw silk to cope with the trend of world economic decline. There are also various related aspects that work together in a mutually reinforcing cycle, which is why the current situation exists. Our country is not like this. Most of the authorities in charge, except for a few, cannot make the finished products adapt to the needs of the world trend. The cost cannot be reduced as the economy declines. They always hope for government assistance. At this time of national treasury emptiness, how can they always provide this kind of relief! I deeply hope that the authorities in charge of the silk industry will make a decision. Now I will briefly state my humble opinions below for correction by those in charge.

As an international commodity, and a clothing product, under the world economic situation, it is not easy to increase the price of goods. Now, the only way is to reduce costs and improve quality under the falling silk prices, in order to increase the export volume.

Those who are engaged in sericulture, from mulberry cultivation and silkworm rearing to raw silk sales, should all follow the above principles to seek the revitalization of the sericulture industry itself. This is the key point. As for how to produce cheap and high-quality raw silk? I have discussed it in detail in the article "Discussion on Modern Silk Industry Issues in Our Country" in the second issue of the second volume of the International Trade Guide. Now I will state my new feelings below: 1. Raw Material Cocoon Quality Issue: The quality of raw silk largely depends on whether the quality of raw material cocoons is uniform or not. In the past, Chinese silkworm cocoon varieties were mixed and of poor quality, resulting in poor finished products and large reeling waste. In the future, we hope to use excellent, suitable, and unified as the principle. Now there is a sericulture joint control committee in Jiangsu and Zhejiang to handle this matter, and the future is promising.

2. Silkworm Cocoon Trading Issue: 75% of the cost of raw silk is the cocoon cost. Therefore, to reduce the cost of raw silk, it is not effective if the cocoon cost is not low. At a time when silk prices are falling and futures sales are decreasing, it is extremely risky for silk factories to conduct fresh cocoon trading, and farmers and silkworm breeders are misled by the occasional rise in cocoon prices. It is better to switch to dry cocoon trading, using the current silk price as the standard to calculate the dry cocoon price, so that both sericulture and silk reeling parties can share the benefits and bear the harm together. The entire sericulture industry maintains an attitude of coexistence and co-prosperity. However, this kind of dry cocoon trading is that the silkworm breeders sell the dry cocoons directly to the silk factories, which is definitely not the dry cocoon trading between the surplus cocoon merchants and silk factories currently practiced in Jiangsu and Zhejiang. However, there are still two points to consider when conducting dry cocoon trading: 1. Silkworm cocoon drying and storage require machinery, technology, hygiene, and appropriate warehouses, which cannot be undertaken by the silkworm farmers themselves. Under the current situation, it is necessary to use cooperative methods to establish organizations for dry storage cooperation, and the government should stand in a guiding and assisting position. 2. In recent years, in the era of low prices of agricultural products, the farmers' economy is extremely difficult. It is not possible for the current economic situation of farmers to store the cocoons obtained from sericulture for a long time and wait for a good price. It seems that it is not effective to conduct dry cocoon mortgages. It is difficult for current banks to handle these small dry cocoon mortgages. It is better for the previous cooperatives to handle the mortgages. However, how can the cooperatives have such huge funds? It is hoped that the government will guarantee the cooperatives to borrow money from the banks and then conduct dry cocoon mortgages, which seems easier.

3. Mechanical Transformation Issue: If there are excellent and uniform raw materials, to obtain uniform raw silk production, it is necessary to have proper processing. In this processing process, some rely entirely on the skilled technology of female workers, such as the Gunze system factories in Japan; some rely on the assistance of excellent machinery, such as the Katakura system factories in Japan. Considering the current situation of silk factories in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, it is not easy to use skilled female workers with new technologies to produce high-quality raw silk. It is easier to achieve results by using the assistance of excellent machinery, such as the rapid efficiency of silk factories in Hangzhou, Jiaxing, and Huzhou. It is hoped that silk merchants in Jiangsu and Zhejiang will rise up and switch to using slow-speed multi-end machines. (After testing this type of machine in a silk factory in Hangzhou, I strongly urged silk factories in Jiangsu and Zhejiang to switch to it.)

4. Management Reform Issue: In the past, silk factories in Jiangsu and Zhejiang mostly operated on a small scale, and the management methods were very outdated. In the future, they should refer to the following principles to implement reforms:

1. Operators must make long-term plans; 2. Efforts should be made to improve equipment and technology for increasing raw silk production; 3. Strengthen training for employees directly involved in production, and pay attention to their hygiene protection and education; 4. Save expenses and provide preferential treatment to producers; 5. Producers and sellers should cooperate to facilitate large-scale direct exports.

On China's Silk Industry Control Policy by Zong Fan 186

The Inevitability of Silk Industry Control

China's silk industry, since being oppressed by the Japanese silk industry and affected by the international economic panic in the most recent years, with the disastrous fall in prices and the reduction in export figures, has suffered a tragedy unprecedented in the history of its silk industry. The closure of silk factories everywhere, not to mention the losses of sericultural farmers, with eight or nine out of ten going bankrupt due to losses, and those who committed suicide themselves or even their whole families were also common occurrences. This was last year's cocoon harvest.

What is the situation this year? There is no definite report yet; but it can be predicted that farmers' sericulture is even more unprofitable, and silk factories are struggling in hardship.

Is there no hope for China's silk industry after all? That's not entirely true. Take Japan as an example: their natural climate and the quality of silkworm cocoons are not as good as China's, and their labor costs are two or three times higher than China's. But they can barely maintain because of the consistent spirit from top to bottom, unifying silkworm varieties, reducing production costs, consistent raw material cocoon silk reeling capacity, and improving raw silk sales control. In simple terms: it is to maximize the scientific nature of technology and fully control management, so although silk prices have decreased, the number of ports can still be maintained considerably.

In China, although there are many natural endowments, there is no organization and no scientific basis in all aspects of sericulture, silk reeling, and sales. To seek the revival and development of the silk industry, there is naturally only one way out, which is to exert the full power of the government and unite all aspects of agriculture, industry, and commerce regarding all planting, breeding, sericulture, cocoon sales, silk reeling, and even foreign trade, whether technical or economic, and move forward from the policy of control.

The Origin of Economic Control Policies 187

Economic control policies are now not only applied to the silk industry, but also to all other industries and all other countries 丨丨 whether it is the Soviet Union, a socialist country, the United Kingdom and the United States, capitalist countries, or Italy, which is ruled by a pan-fascist party, they all have to adopt this kind of policy.

Before the Soviet Russian socialist economic policy was successful and before the world economic panic was fully intensified, the entire world economy was dominated by the consistent ideas of Adam Smith's free economy. His slogan was: "Develop production, obtain profits, accumulate personal wealth, to increase the country's resources." Because of the domination of this economic thought, on a small scale, there was a laissez-faire economic organization within the country, and on a large scale, free trade regulations were established in the world. However, after the extreme development of capitalism and the increasingly fierce economic competition between countries, the unprecedented great war in Europe arose from this. At the same time, due to the occurrence of cartels, trusts, and industrial rationalization movements, small controls were formed in each industrial sector, suppressing the majority of the working masses internally and fighting head-on with other capitalist countries externally. In the mutual infighting, the flaws of capitalism gradually became exposed, and an unprecedented world economic panic occurred.

The production of the controlled economic movement is the liquidation of the past laissez-faireism, putting all industries under orderly and planned control, with the entire country as a group, internally combining capital and labor, creating a self-sufficient world, and externally preventing the harm of various countries, or using this force to oppress small groups. This controlled economic plan movement, the pan-ideological Italy, had already promulgated laws in 1926 and was proceeding step by step. And since the Soviet Union implemented the Five-Year Plan in 1927, its excellent achievements have shocked all countries in the world!

Regarding the silk industry, the organization of the Silk Industry Improvement Committee in Italy and the implementation of various control methods in Japan have all achieved significant results.

The Future Trend of China's Silk Industry Control 188

Under the current situation in China, to require the improvement of mulberry gardens, the unification of silkworm varieties, the reduction of cocoon prices, the superior quality of silk, and the increase in market prices, it is naturally necessary for all aspects of agriculture, industry, and commerce to make planned, systematic, and step-by-step progress under the guidance and supervision of the government.

In the past one or two years, the governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces have indeed been proceeding in the direction mentioned above. This year, they have also reorganized the Jiangsu and Zhejiang Silk Industry Control Committee, and it is heard that they have decided on considerable steps and are preparing to make active progress.

However, we hope that the government and people in the silk industry will not forget the interests of the farmers, the most central force of the silk industry, when carrying out the controlled economic movement! The Russian controlled economic policy, of course, seeks the welfare of the entire people, without any personal intentions. Even the most important goal of the Italian pan-fascist controlled economic movement is to stop and hinder the production of capitalist factories; to increase the profits of all workers; and to ban the exorbitant profits of banks and exchanges. In short, the purpose of this controlled economic movement is to use the entire national power to revitalize industry internally, resist aggression externally, and, on the one hand, to revive the collapsing rural economy, and on the other hand, to resist foreign silk industry competition. Therefore, it is necessary to seek the interests of the entire silk industry, and it must not be for the benefit of a few factory owners and a few breeding experts!

In the past, the high price sale of improved silkworm varieties made it impossible for those who could not afford to buy them to enjoy the benefits. Farmers in Yuhang and Lin'an, Zhejiang, opposed the new breeding methods. Although according to the official report, old-style breeding merchants were stirring up trouble, the implementers' spirit failed to make the people understand, and they cannot but resign their responsibility. And the recent restriction on cocoon prices, although it is also an unavoidable measure. But if we cannot first fundamentally plan the cost of sericulture for farmers and make an overall plan for farmers' lives, simply suppressing prices is still harming the people. It is still a long way from the modern so-called new economic movement 丨丨 controlled economic movement. The so-called improvement of the silk industry will become a mere term.

Lessons from Japan's Silk Industry Control by Yu 189

China, known as the ancestor of the silk industry, has recently been unable to live up to its reputation of more than four thousand years of history, and it has been in a slump. However, the silk industry of Japan, a small island country, has leapt to the first place in the world in terms of both production and trade. The reason why the Japanese have such a position is definitely not due to luck or chance, but due to decades of struggle and effort. This article intends to give a brief description of Japan's silk control for the reference of our silk cocoon industry.

1. Control to Improve Silk Quality

In the early Meiji period, in order to prevent crude manufacturing and compete with advanced countries such as France and Italy, the government adopted the following controls to improve quality: 1. The silk industry established raw silk inspection stations by the state to inspect exported raw silk, and each province and county government and silk industry association also established raw silk inspection agencies. 2. Sericulture (A) The silkworm industry control office and silkworm seed industry association, etc., forcibly implemented silkworm seed inspection. (B) In terms of silkworm seed and breeding methods, 1. Establish a silkworm industry experiment station, 2. Subsidize young silkworm joint breeding centers and joint mulberry gardens, etc., 3. The public automatically organizes silkworm seed sub-farms to operate and specially contract associations, etc.

2. Control of Scaling Up

The control of scaled-up management is to make up for the following shortcomings of small-scale management in the silk industry with combinations, joint facilities, and other legal controls. 1. Crude manufacturing and abuse of trust; 2. There is often a danger of overproduction, resulting in the disastrous fall of silk and cocoon prices due to reckless sales, which is no different from suicide; 3. Cannot have the ability to control market prices like large-scale enterprises; market prices often fluctuate; 4. Lack of control among peers, resulting in the inability to share the benefits of large-scale transactions such as jointly obtaining raw materials and selling products; 5. There is an intermediary profit between purchasing raw materials and selling products. Recently, small-scale operators; on the one hand, are oppressed by capital, and on the other hand, are sacrificed by the fall in silk prices. To avoid this pain, it is necessary to have a joint sericulture section to briefly explain as follows:

(1) Silk Reeling Industry (A) Organized according to government laws, such as industrial combination silk reeling. It was opened in the tenth year of the Meiji era. At that time, manual silk reelers (i.e., silkworm farmers) jointly invested in silk reeling in order to reach a certain export volume, which is called group silk reeling. In the 33rd year of the Meiji era, the Industrial Combination Law was promulgated, giving various groups a legal basis. The government also gave tax exemption preferential treatment and gave various financial conveniences. The silk reeling method has also changed from manual to machine. At the same time, it contains the exclusion of intermediaries and the oppression of silk reelers by silkworm farmers. In the second year of the Showa era, the combination silk reeling industry established the Japan Raw Silk Sales Combination Federation, which sells the raw silk of the combination directly to exporters. Recently, it announced an expansion plan, wanting to increase from the current annual production capacity of 22,000 dan to 44,000 dan within five years, and it is expected to establish a sales office in New York from the tenth year of the Showa era to trade directly with the United States. (B) The government sets subsidies to promote the development of the silk reeling industry. For example, the provisional meeting in the seventh year of the Showa era resolved to pay a reward of 2.6 million yuan in ten years. The first 120,000 yuan has been paid in the seventh year of the Showa era. (C) Organized by the person concerned automatically, such as the Japan Silk Association, etc. (D) Restricted by law, stipulating the minimum limit for newly established businesses; the Silk Reeling Industry Law promulgated in September and implemented in October of the seventh year of the Showa era stipulates that the mechanical manufacturing industry must be approved by the Minister of Agriculture and Forestry, and a newly established mechanical factory must have at least 150 ends, otherwise it will not be approved.

(2) Sericulture (A) Those organized according to the laws promulgated by the government include sericulture associations, silkworm seed industry associations, etc. Its business is to unify silkworm species, guide sericulture, inspect cocoons, improve cocoon trading methods, prevent silkworm diseases, mediate sericulture disputes, and improve other aspects of sericulture. (B) The government subsidizes the joint cocoon warehouse organized by the industrial association. The purpose is to stabilize cocoon prices, implement large-scale dry cocoon storage, and prevent silkworm farmers from selling due to financial difficulties. According to the investigation, there are already 65 groups that have received government subsidies in the seventh year of the Showa era. In addition, it pre-lends money. (C) The person concerned automatically initiates and implements the sub-farm management method. (D) Restricted by law, stipulating the minimum limit for newly established silkworm seed businesses. The detailed rules for the implementation of the Silk Industry Law in the fourth year of the Showa era stipulate that the silkworm seed industry must have certain equipment and must not be less than 100,000 moths per year. Otherwise, it will not be allowed to be established.

3. Control of Enterprise and Raw Material Monopoly

Since the silk reeling industry has separated from the sericulture industry and developed into an independent industry. The most concerned about the silk reelers is how to obtain cheap and beautiful raw materials. Especially since the area of origin, although the silk price has fallen, the silk output has not decreased, but the profit has been reduced. In order to maintain their past position, the silk reelers, on the one hand, try to improve silk reeling technology and increase silk reeling efficiency, and at the same time, they are more concerned about beautiful raw materials to seek silk quality improvement. Therefore, the silk reelers and silkworm farmers signed a special contract, monopolizing the purchase of raw material cocoons, and the silk reeling industry itself controlled the quality of the cocoons. There are three ways to control: 1. Lending cash to silkworm farmers in advance to prevent farmers from selling the cocoons to outsiders. 2. Make silkworm farmers breed special varieties that are most beneficial to the silk reelers, and 3. Dispatch sericulture instructors to teach certain feeding methods to ensure silk quality improvement. In the third year of the Showa era, the number of silk reeling factories that signed special contracts was 207, and the number of special contract sericulture households was 84.

Recently, the silk price is not a rise in price, but a fundamental fall. Therefore, how to stop the silk price from falling is the most urgent problem for the silk industry at present. The author's control methods:

(1) Silk Price (A) The silk industry jointly cooperates to restrict the sale at a price below a certain level, and prohibits futures market transactions to prevent speculators from manipulating the market, such as the resolutions of the Silk Central Association and the Silk Congress, which can restrict production and pre-lend money for sale at a good price. (B) Banks, etc., give special financial accommodation to silk industry groups, but in order to force the implementation of silk price business, they stop lending money due to silk reeling. (C) The government comes forward to compensate the silk industry for losses, and mediates with banks for the silk industry to obtain loans, and then the government purchases raw silk to raise silk prices.

(2) Cocoon Price (A) The government provides low-interest loans to silkworm farmers to supply basic emergency needs, and issues subsidies to establish cocoon warehouses and joint dry cocoon storage warehouses. (B) The prefectural roads and governments lend money to cocoon markets, cocoon warehouses, and sericulture associations, etc.

Generally speaking, the current Japanese silk control law is limited to the four types listed above. Among them, the first and second items have the most significant results. And the reason why there are such results is partly due to the government's promotion, subsidies, and subsidies, and partly due to the people's automatic organization. The future development is in full swing. Looking back at our country, I can't help but feel cold.

Securities and Public Bonds Were Most Vigorous on Saturday 193

Last week (May 29th to June 3rd) in the securities market, Monday was a holiday for the summer festival, and the market was closed for one day. There were only five days of trading, and the trading volume was quite considerable. Although there were a few speculators who wanted to take advantage of the situation due to the northern armistice, it did not hinder the overall situation. The market trading volume and the number of accounts reached more than 30 million, so any slight changes in the situation were enough to cause waves. On Tuesday, the armistice conference was inconclusive, and Feng Yuxiang’s army's attitude made people suspicious. Various firms continued to sell, and the market price fell by one yuan. On Wednesday, the news was dull, and the market saw both rises and falls. On Thursday, the armistice agreement was signed, and short sellers missed the opportunity. Northern firms covered their short positions, and the financial sector absorbed them. The market price rose by 1.23 yuan. The 20-year disaster relief public bond began trading on this day, but there were very few inquiries, and the market price was extremely stable. On Friday, the price continued to rise by half a yuan due to the slight covering of short positions in 38 and 50 numbers. On Saturday, part of the Japanese army withdrew, and various firms began to cover their short positions on a large scale. The financial sector continued to buy, and northern firms were also very enthusiastic. The market price rose sharply, and various bonds repeatedly reached new highs. The upward trend on this day was the most vigorous of the entire week. The Reorganization bonds approached 60 yuan, and the Consolidated Tax bonds broke through 46 yuan. It is not easy to see a sudden drop in the future for the time being. As a result of the week's market prices, the increase ranged from a little over one yuan to a little over three yuan, of which the increase of 3.20 yuan for the Consolidated Six bonds was the largest. The number of transactions totaled 54.12 million yuan, including 42,000 yuan in spot transactions. In futures, the Consolidated Tax bonds accounted for 21.125 million, Reorganization bonds 8.36 million, 1929 Customs bonds 8.2 million, 1920 and 1929 Customs bonds 11.69 million, and the rest ranged from over 100,000 to several hundred thousand.

Cocoon production is still good, and the overall quality is 60% of a normal year. New cocoons have already entered the market. (Silk Waste Shipments Are Not Smooth) The sales of yellow and white silk waste have been sluggish for a long time, and exports are not smooth. Last week, only 284 pieces were shipped to Marseille and other ports via French mail.

(Artificial Silk Shipments Are Busy) The export of artificial silk is becoming increasingly scarce. Last week, a total of only 245 boxes were shipped to various ports along the Yangtze River, as well as Hangzhou, Shaoxing, Huzhou, and Jiaxing in Zhejiang Province.

Random Notes

The Profession of Spreading Rumors 198

— Cunxin

"Ah, long time no see."

"Ah, long time no see, how are you?" I ran into K, whom I hadn't seen in years, as I came out of the Sincere Company. He had a triangular belt slung across his shoulder, and the round silver badge of a certain division was displayed, making him look valiant and spirited. Who would believe that he was the famous "fair-faced scholar" from school back then? The changes of the world are truly beyond human control.

"Where have you been all this time? Why haven't I heard from you?"

"After we parted, I did a lot of things. I ate chalk dust, wrote brilliant essays that were 'as instructed,' and finally, with the introduction of a friend, I went to work at the headquarters of a certain division. I'm still there. This time, I came to Shanghai for business."

"Very good, serving on the battlefield. That's what a man should do," I said with admiration and encouragement. "So what is your position?" I knew he wouldn't be shooting guns.

"My position is spreading rumors," he said somberly. "What about serving the country?"

"Military life must be very enjoyable, right?" I wondered why he seemed so depressed.

"Enjoyable? When we're on the move, of course, it's very enjoyable. Wearing the skin of a tyrant, who would dare say 'no'? For example, when our troops arrive in a village and want a few cows or a few girls, it doesn't take much effort. But there are also painful times. Even when we've clearly suffered a defeat, we have to tell people that we killed the enemy bravely, advanced several miles, and captured so many spoils of war. Even when we're clearly retreating, we have to say it's 'for strategic reasons, so...' etc. At this time, the secretary has to think very hard. You see, what we see is the truth, but what we have to say has to be a lie. It's like putting on a smiling face when you're wounded. This pain is hard to bear. I really don't know where the truth has gone. Sometimes, I wonder if I'm dreaming. Alas, I curse this profession of spreading rumors!"

"Hmm, the profession of spreading rumors..."

The Case of the Two County Magistrates 199

— Geng

As the war at the Great Wall began, with a few bangs and crashes of gunfire, the enemy was able to enter the hall and room, and press close to the capital region (this capital region is naturally the old stuff). Speaking from a military perspective, our side, because it was in the vicinity of the suburbs of Tianjin and Beiping, had already set up a "predetermined new defense line". The various defending armies, for "military strategy reasons", had no choice but to retreat rapidly, in order to achieve the concentrated formation of the "predetermined new defense line". Therefore, the enemy's ability to follow and advance was not because of their victorious attacks, but rather our side's respectful demonstration of peaceful sincerity, and the winning strategy of seeking benevolence and gaining benevolence. Helplessly, the civil officials ultimately couldn't see through the mysteries of the military officials. Feng Chengdi, the county magistrate of Tongxian, a vital town in eastern Hebei (only 40 li away from Beiping), was as foolish as a country bumpkin who didn't understand how a revolving lantern works. He dared to mistakenly believe that the national army had fought a losing battle, so he implemented the best of the thirty-six stratagems and ran away into the depths of the white clouds, leaving people unaware of his whereabouts for as long as a week.

Following this, the chief of the public security bureau, the director of the finance bureau, the county party headquarters, and other important personnel in other important organs, naturally imitated and enjoyed congratulating each other on the "joy of moving house". As a result, no one was in charge of the city, the order was in chaos, and the prisoners in the prison also took the opportunity to break out and escape. Chairman He, the chairman of the military sub-committee, then appointed a new county magistrate, Zhang Qijun, to come to Tongxian to take office. Just as the new county magistrate was beginning to carry out the first step of his virtuous policy of "stabilizing the people's hearts and restoring commerce", it was suddenly discovered that the old county magistrate was also continuing to work as usual in Sanjianfang, 20 li west of Beiping. From then on, with a sudden crash, the strange tale of the "case of the two county magistrates" spread far and wide, and the confusing and elusive "double envelope case" would also lose its exclusive right from this point forward.

This case was discovered on May 25th. "Monks have their own sutras, Taoists have their own books." It is said that it has not yet been resolved. I will rashly set up a joint trial court, and also take on the duties of a lawyer entrusted by both parties, and am willing to provide free defense as follows.

On the plaintiff's side, the county magistrate is the ruler of a county, and his every move is related to the governance or chaos of the area, and the safety or danger of the people. In this serious situation, the responsibility should be increased, and he should "die in his duty" and not abandon the city and run away. Now that the new county magistrate has been ordered to come here to take office, the old county magistrate should quickly transfer all seals, files, and especially the silver and funds, and immediately hand them over properly, and await thorough investigation and handling, etc.

On the defendant's side, the old county magistrate's term had not yet expired, and the new county magistrate suddenly came to take office, which violated regulations. The responsibility should be borne by the other party. Furthermore, the old county magistrate, in order to preserve the important documents of the county government, so as to maintain tax revenue in the future, had no choice but to avoid the dangerous city and temporarily work at the "new location" of Sanjianfang. This was originally a "predetermined plan" and not a hasty escape. He was planning to return to the county government within a few days to clean up the remaining matters, but unexpectedly, the superiors did not investigate and suddenly appointed a new official, which disappointed my hard work. It is hoped that Lord He will have foresight, withdraw the order, then the locality will be fortunate, and I will be fortunate, etc.

Listening to these two lawyers' free defense, which is "well-founded and reasonable", it can be seen that this "case of the two county magistrates" is ultimately not like the dispute in the "double envelope case", which can be resolved with a single look in the demon-revealing mirror. However, there is nothing in the world that cannot be resolved. Even the dangerous situation in Tianjin and Beiping is like this. One side said "determined to take it" and the other side said "betting everything on the city", but in fact, haven't both sides already been tip-toeing around, like a lonely widower and a grieving widow, privately resolving their matters?

Seeing so many red-lacquered chamber pots lined up in front of every household every morning, how can one not sigh three times at China's "thriving population"?

After the January 28th Incident, in the rubble of Baoshan Road, Qiujiang Road, and Gongxing Road in Zhabei, one can often see people from Jiangbei burying their heads in "treasure hunting"!

On the night before every new moon and full moon, there is bound to be the cry of Pudong women selling long ingots. Then, paper ashes can be seen scattered on the roads. A group of old-timers immediately organize themselves into "volunteer street cleaners", taking small dung baskets to sweep the ingot ashes clean. In the "free urination areas" in Shanghai's alleys, there are often notices from the Municipal Council: "Urinating in this area is prohibited. Violators will be sent to the police for investigation." But it has no effect whatsoever.

School Life Sketches 201

— Meihua

"Old Huang, have you got a lot of bedbugs on your bed these days?"

"Hmph! How could I not have a lot? Look, my whole body is covered in itchy welts. It's really annoying!" Little Zhang lifted up his sleeves and showed Old Huang his skin, covered in red and purple patches.

"A lot? I've got even more!" Old Huang showed off his artistic skin in the same way.

In our school, because it's been hot these days, and there are so many students living on campus, and the dormitory facilities are so simple and unhygienic, the annoying bedbugs are rampant in the beds and mats. The above is a conversation between two students about the rampant bedbugs.

Old Huang and Little Zhang talked for a while, and inspired by the poetry, he couldn't help but pick up a piece of chalk and write a sleeping poem on the blackboard. The poem goes:

"Spring sleep doesn't know dawn, bedbugs bite everywhere; the sound of scratching at night, how many itchy welts do you know?"

Old Huang laughed first, and then Little Zhang also laughed. They even forgot the pain caused by all the bedbugs on their bodies and laughed!

Eulogy for the Transition of Spring and Summer 202

— Kuangbei

Spring has already slipped away amid the unexpected cold. The atmosphere of human affairs seems to have been affected by it. This year's spring is so abnormal! Continuous spring rains and unexpected spring chills almost entirely occupied a period of this spring. Now it is "flowers fall and water flows, spring departs," leaving only a poet's heart of remembrance. No, it only offers the opportunity for liberation, regardless of the boys who come to dance. As for me, feeling the arrival of summer, in this "the spring scenery is gone, who knows where" situation, the weather is gradually turning hot. Lying in a room like a steamer, I won't be able to breathe, and it will lower my efficiency - that's no fun.

However, these are ultimately small matters. We must open our eyes and look at the prelude ahead:

The unlucky spring did not bring us the bright spring we hoped for. The gentle spring breeze and lovely spring scenery, at the beginning of its opening, brought the bad news of the enemy's further encroachment and, in a gloomy atmosphere, took away our naturally fortified Jehol Province. Are we to blame the generals who guarded the land for not trying their best? That is unavoidable injustice. Heaven's will is already so favorable to them and unfavorable to us. What more can be said?

Now summer has arrived. History tells us that China can not only be called "Zhina" but also "Huaxia." There was an ancient fool who passed his home three times without entering - the Xia Dynasty's Yu the Great - who diligently settled the mountains and rivers, obtaining vast plains and a beautiful land, but which was treated by later generations like a piece of stinking, rotten meat, worthless, ceded piece by piece to others, developing into a world where "barbarians corrupt China."

Now summer has arrived. "The scorching sun in the sky" is summer's only characteristic, and it also symbolizes "the tyrant's sun is upon us." I hear that when the scorching sun is in the sky, young gentlemen and ladies have electric fans to drive away the heat, and are lazily unconcerned. The poor masses can also take off their shirts and take a round fan, and "flap, flap" to make wind, so it is not difficult to breathe a cool breath. However, "the tyrant's sun is upon us," what plan will be made?

What I am most concerned about are the officials, the wealthy elders, and in this summer's divine arrival, even with electric fans at their side, they can't help but shout repeatedly: "Hot, hot, hot!" So, there will be elegant acts of seeking secluded places to escape the heat, which will be enough to relax the chest, broaden the mind, and prolong life. Beidaihe, Yangquan, Jehol... all of these are beautiful summer resorts. Now that these beautiful rivers and mountains have mostly fallen into the hands of the enemy, how can we not sigh helplessly, "where to escape the summer?" Lushan, Guling, and Moganshan will probably hang up "full" signs. Qingdao is still acceptable, but Qinhuangdao is also impossible to go to.

Now summer has arrived, and in this opening month of May for summer, even leaf by leaf of bloody history is churning. "May Third," "May Seventh," "May Ninth," "May Thirtieth," were all gifts of this summer, ornaments of the season. The people of the country must not forget them. I hear that they are going to hold mournful commemorations. The ordinary, idle officials will have to bother, bother, to bow three times before the portrait of our Premier, and maybe there will be a sorrowful sermon.

The schools will still have holidays according to regulations. The students and compatriots who shout the loudest for national salvation will be overjoyed by three hundred, unable to contain their joy. Dancing can be linked to national salvation, and XX can also be linked to national salvation. Look, the carousing and dancing, movies and amusements at sea, how much will they turn the opportunity and develop their businesses because of this.

A eulogy says: "What does the country have to do with me? What need is there to save it? Would it not be better to rest?"
